## Station 1: Airport Terminal 1

**Page ID:** 5120
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Airport_Terminal_1

**Summary:**
Stepford Airport Terminal 1 (also known as Terminal 1 ) is an underground through station in the Airport Zone .

**Full Content:**

Airport Terminal 1 Entrance Interior Platform View Concourse Arrivals & Departures Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone SAO C Station headcode Dispatching - No Electrification Line Yes Airport Branch Station Information Location Farleigh District Zone Airport Zone Platforms 1 Tracks 1 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes & ticket office available Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Stepford Airport Central 0.74 miles / 1.19 kilometres Airport Terminal 3 0.42 miles / 676 metres Airport Terminal 2 1.14 miles / 1.83 kilometres Track Layout to Airport Terminal 2 or Airport Terminal 3 from Stepford Airport Central Stepford Airport Terminal 1 (also known as Terminal 1 ) is an underground through station in the Airport Zone . It is served by AirLink services to Airport Terminal 2 and Airport Terminal 3 . Terminal 1 is a single-platform unidirectional station; trains from this station travel towards Terminal 3 and Terminal 2 only. History [ ] 2019 1 February - Version 1.1.9 Airport Terminal 1 added to the network as part of the Airport Terminals and is an underground AirLink through station with 1 platform. Trains cannot return from Airport Terminal 2 as it is unidirectional. New routes: R052 & R053 2022 19 June Sneak peek for Airport Terminal 1's overhaul was released. Don't feel blue, we have an upgraded station for you... 27 August - Version 1.10 Station overhauled with a new station building. Resembles Heathrow Terminal 4 station . Shops were added outside the platforms instead of a black wall at the exit. Airport Terminal 1 is no longer dispatchable. New routes: R058 & R060 2023 17 July - Version 1.10.8 Class 80x stop markers added to Platform 1. Trivia [ ] The name is based on Heathrow's terminal stations, but Heathrow Terminals 2 and 3 are served by the same station. The latest station model resembles Heathrow Terminal 4 station . This is the second station to have one track and one platform. The first is Newry Harbour , the third is Leighton West and the fourth is Carnalea Bridge . This station is also one of the two stations to be through stations with single platforms, the other being Carnalea Bridge . However, Newry Harbour had another platform added in V1.9 . The CIS Boards at this station used to not function properly. Prior to V1.10, passengers wishing to go to Airport Terminal 3 or Stepford Airport Central had to change at Airport Terminal 2 , while passengers coming from Airport Terminal 3 or Airport Terminal 2 will have had to change at Stepford Airport Central in order to disembark at this station. Now, trains can travel from this station to Airport Terminal 3 directly. However, you still can not get to this station from another terminal without changing, as it is still unidirectional. Strangely, this station, which is located underground, has no entrance connecting to the ground level. Players spawning at this station would spawn directly at the concourse just before the ticket gate. This trait was formerly also shared with Airport Terminal 2 . However, when the stations in the former Airport Zone were given overhauls in V1.10 , Terminal 2 received a road connection. This station has step-free access. This station looked like Airport Terminal 2 when it was under construction. The only way to get to them would be track walking, which is considered trespassing . Trains from Leighton Stepford Road cannot call at this station. Passengers would need to disembark at Stepford Airport Central then change trains to get to this station if arriving from Leighton Stepford Road . Prior to V1.10 , this station was quite far from Airport Terminal 2 and drivers were often late when they arrived there. In addition, there was also a 75 MPH speed limit which meant drivers were often speeding in order to not be late. Compared to the distance from Stepford Airport Central to Airport Terminal 2 , the time it took from this station to Airport Terminal 2 was about 3√ó as long. When the overhaul sneak peek of this station was released, it received criticism for a bland design, with the blue uplights being repetitive. This station was dispatchable before V1.10 , probably due to Terminal 1 being a small station compared to other stations in Stepford Airport. Before V1.10 , there was no concourse for this station, instead there was just a wall placed there. After V1.10, a concourse was added with shops and access to departures and exits, though those end with an invisible wall with no actual access to the surface or terminal. If you manage to align your camera correctly so that you can look outside of the station, you can see that the "exits" lead into the void. At the concourse, there are 2 restaurants next to each other that seem to be in fierce competition named " Come eat pizza with us! " and " My pizza is better than yours, Billy ". This is the only station with multilingual signs, written in English, French and Spanish. This station is the only station in-game to have no access to the outside. The advertisement displayed above the station's entrance At the entrance of the station, an advert that is only displayed at this station, states "fast, direct, regular services to Stepford Central ". However, there are no direct services to Stepford Central from this station. The double variants of the Class 397 and Class 802 are too long for the platforms here, having their last 2 coaches off the platform. Gallery [ ] Airport Terminal 1 under construction Sneak peek of the overhauled Airport Terminal 1, published on 19 June 2022 Pre V1.10 station Stations Stepford Central ‚Ä¢ Stepford East ‚Ä¢ St Helens Bridge ‚Ä¢ Elsemere Junction ‚Ä¢ Berrily ‚Ä¢ Morganstown ‚Ä¢ Stepford Airport Parkway ‚Ä¢ Stepford Airport Central ‚Ä¢ Airport Terminal 1 ‚Ä¢ Airport Terminal 2 ‚Ä¢ Airport Terminal 3 ‚Ä¢ Water Newton ‚Ä¢ Leighton Stepford Road List of Stations ‚Ä¢ List of Stations (Statistics) ‚Ä¢ List of Station Codes Upcoming stations are marked in italics , former stations are marked in strikethrough . ## Station 2: Airport Terminal 2

**Page ID:** 2449
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Airport_Terminal_2

**Summary:**
Stepford Airport Terminal 2 (also known as Terminal 2 ) is a terminus past Stepford Airport Central , trains will also turn around here to Terminal 3 . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Stepford Victoria and St Helens Bridge ; Waterline services to Newry ; AirLink services to Stepford Central , Airport Terminal 3 and Leighton Stepford Road ; and AirLink Shuttle services to Stepford Airport Parkway .

**Full Content:**

Airport Terminal 2 Entrance Interior Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone SAX C Station headcode Dispatching X Yes (1 slot) P1-4 Electrification Line Yes Airport Branch Station Information Location Farleigh District Zone Airport Zone Platforms 4 Tracks 4 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts and ramps Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Airport Terminal 1 1.14 miles / 1.83 kilometres [ note 1 ] Airport West 1.2 miles / 1.93 kilometres Stepford Airport Central 1.33 miles / 2.14 kilometres Terminus Airport Terminal 3 0.95 miles / 1.53 kilometres Preceding depot Following depot Farleigh Depot (Road 17) - Stepford Airport Terminal 2 (also known as Terminal 2 ) is a terminus past Stepford Airport Central , trains will also turn around here to Terminal 3 . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Stepford Victoria and St Helens Bridge ; Waterline services to Newry ; AirLink services to Stepford Central , Airport Terminal 3 and Leighton Stepford Road ; and AirLink Shuttle services to Stepford Airport Parkway . This station opened on 1 February 2019 along with Airport Terminal 1 , and was refurbished in Version 1.10 . History [ ] 2019 26 January Sneak peek for Airport Terminal 2 was released. 1 February - Version 1.1.9 Airport Terminal 2 added to the network as part of the Airport Terminals, as an underground AirLink terminus with 3 platforms. Based on Heathrow Terminals 2 & 3 on the London Underground. Trains terminating at Platform 1 do not turn around when returning to Stepford Central . New routes: R052 & R053 2 February - Version 1.1.10 Added AirLink services to Airport Terminal 3 . New route: R055 16 September - Version 1.3.26 ( Five Million Update ) Added AirLink services to Leighton Stepford Road . New route: R057 2022 3 July Sneak peek for Airport Terminal 2's overhaul was released. Trains, planes, and another instalment for #SneakPeekSundays 27 August - Version 1.10 Station overhauled, new station building and is now located above ground. Based on Manchester Airport . Introduced "Turnaround mid-route" functionality. Platforms increased from 3 to 4; all platforms can now serve as through and terminal platforms, with the aformentioned feature. The platform allocation is randomised. The terminus loop, similar to the Port Benton Loop , was removed. Added Stepford Connect services to Stepford Victoria and Benton (via SAP ) . Added Waterline services to the Newry branch and Benton (via SAW ) . New routes: R017 , R046 , R058 , R059 & R060 2023 2 April - Version 1.10.7 New route: R048 Trivia [ ] The revamped Airport Terminal 2 is based on Manchester Airport in real life. [ 1 ] The pre- V1.10 station may have been based on Heathrow Terminals 2 & 3 on the London Underground. The station's name resembles Heathrow Airport's terminal stations, however, Heathrow Terminals 1, 2, and 3 are served by the same station. This station has the most platforms among the three terminals, having 4 platforms. Prior to V1.10 , it still had the most platforms, having 3 platforms, with Airport Terminal 1 having 1 and Airport Terminal 3 having 2. This station was made dispatchable due to player demand. The CIS Boards at this station used to not function properly. This station, along with Airport Terminal 1 , used to have no exit. It was located underneath a purple airport terminal building with an ATC tower. It could be seen if you zoomed out far enough when driving a train. The building of Airport Terminal 2 and the ATC tower were also visible from James Street prior to its revamp. Before this station was opened, it had one platform, similar to Airport Terminal 1 . There are no trains to Airport Terminal 1 serving this station. In order to go to Airport Terminal 1 station from this station, passengers will need to take a train to Stepford Airport Central and then change to another train that goes via Terminal 1. This also applies to Airport Terminal 3. Airport Terminal 2 (X), as well as Farleigh (J), Esterfield (Q), Leighton West (K), and Airport Terminal 3 (Z), do not have a letter in their name that is their station headcode . Along with Airport Terminal 3 and Edgemead , this station is one of the three having the "Turnaround mid-route" functionality. This station is the second Waterline - AirLink interchange , the first being Morganstown . [ note 2 ] This station is one of the three triple-line junctions, the others being Berrily and Leighton Stepford Road . Additionally, this is the only triple-line station that is not served by Stepford Express . Despite being an airport terminal station, its scenery has little to no resemblance of an airport. It instead consists of many buildings and skyscrapers. The actual "airport terminal" is a short walk from this station. It is possible that this station additionally serves accommodation, as the "Cozy Palace Hotel" is nearby. "Cozy Palace Hotel" is likely named after " Crowne Plaza hotel ", a hotel chain that can be found near airports across the world. Between V1.10.0 and V1.10.6, this used to be the second Stepford Connect station that the Class 68 and the Class 444 couldn't serve. The first one is Houghton Rake . In V1.10.7, a new route ( R048 ( from St Helens Bridge )) was added, allowing the two trains to serve this station. This is the only station in the whole SCR network where all Aventra trains (present in the game) can go: AirLink Shuttle Class 345 , Waterline Class 730 /0, and Stepford Connect Class 720 and 730/1. The tunnel that links Farleigh TMD (Road 2) and James Street passes under this station. There is a StepAir plane roundabout between Farleigh TMD and Airport Terminal 2. The Farleigh Portal Access is located near this station, near the aforementioned StepAir plane roundabout. This is the only station serviced by Waterline that is managed by AirLink . ## Station 3: Airport Terminal 3

**Page ID:** 4827
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Airport_Terminal_3

**Summary:**
Stepford Airport Terminal 3 (also known as Terminal 3 ) is a stub station in the Airport Zone .

**Full Content:**

Airport Terminal 3 Terminal Entrance Car Park Entrance Side Entrance Interior Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone SAZ C Station headcode Dispatching Z Yes (1 slot) P1-3 Electrification Line Yes Airport Branch Station Information Location Farleigh District Zone Airport Zone Platforms 3 Tracks 3 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts and ramps Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Airport Terminal 1 0.4 mi / 0.6 km [ note 1 ] Airport Terminal 2 0.8 mi / 1.3 km [ note 2 ] Terminus Airport Terminal 2 0.8 mi / 1.3 km [ note 3 ] Stepford Airport Terminal 3 (also known as Terminal 3 ) is a stub station in the Airport Zone . It is served by AirLink services to Stepford Central and Leighton Stepford Road as well as by AirLink Shuttle services to Airport Terminal 2 , which reverse ends at this station. This station was opened on 2 February 2019, and was refurbished in Version 1.10 . History [ ] 2019 2 February - Version 1.1.10 Airport Terminal 3 added to the network as part of the Airport Terminals, as an AirLink terminus with an island platform. New route: R055 16 September - Version 1.3.26 ( Five Million Update ) Added AirLink services to Leighton Stepford Road . New route: R057 2022 17 July Sneak peek for Airport Terminal 3's overhaul was released. Pillars, pillars, and yet more pillars for this instalment of #SneakPeekSundays 27 August - Version 1.10 Station overhauled, new station building and has 3 platforms (island platform with a bay platform in the middle). Based on Stansted Airport station . Introduced "Turnaround mid-route" functionality. New routes: R058 & R060 Trivia [ ] Terminal 3 is based on Stansted Airport station [ 1 ] , although its name is based on Heathrow Airport's terminal stations. However, Heathrow Terminals 2 & 3 are served by the same station. The station was not on the SCR Network Map until 17 March 2019. Prior to V1.10 , unlike Airport Terminal 1 and Airport Terminal 2 where their terminal buildings were right above, the red terminal building (probably Terminal 3) was to the west of the station, which was quite far away. This station has step-free access. Passengers must go via Airport Terminal 2 and Stepford Airport Central in order to get from this station to Airport Terminal 1 , as the station only operates in a single direction. Prior to V1.10 , many players criticised this station for being bland in design, as well as it being located in a grass cutting. Many players also thought this station did not look like an airport terminal station. Airport Terminal 3 (Z), as well as Farleigh (J), Leighton West (K), Esterfield (Q) and Airport Terminal 2 (X), do not have a letter in their name that is their station headcode. This station is popular for having drivers starting from here to Leighton Stepford Road ( R057 ) as it has more stops than R056 ( Stepford Airport Central <> Leighton Stepford Road ) . This station and Airport Terminal 2 are the first stations to have the "Turnaround mid-route" functionality. There is a path to the ATC tower nearby, but it is inaccessible. Players can jump above the fences by jumping on top of the door and jump again. This will make the player get into the airport. ## Station 4: Airport West

**Page ID:** 1919
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Airport_West

**Summary:**
Stepford Airport West (also known as Airport West ) is a through station on the Esterfield Branch .

**Full Content:**

Airport West Entrance Interior Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone SAW C Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) P1-2 Electrification Line Yes Esterfield Branch Station Information Location Farleigh District Zone Airport Zone Platforms 2 Tracks 2 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Cambridge Street Parkway 0.9 mi / 1.5 k Airport Terminal 2 1.2 mi / 1.9 km James Street 1.4 mi / 2.3 km Farleigh 1.8 mi / 2.9 km Stepford Airport West (also known as Airport West ) is a through station on the Esterfield Branch . It is served by Waterline to Newry Harbour , Newry , Benton , Airport Terminal 2 , Farleigh and Esterfield . This station provides an out-of-station interchange (OSI) with the nearby Stepford Airport Parkway served by Stepford Connect and AirLink , as mentioned on the station signs. To play these files, consider using another device or convert them into supported formats such as .mp3. History [ ] 2018 13 June Sneak peek for Airport West was released. New entrance 10 December Another sneak peek for Airport West was released, as part of Day 10 of the Advent Calendar. Today's Day 10 sneak peek is another new station, but this one isn't like the others. Airport West is an underground station on Waterline, one stop before James Street. Combined with some lighting updates makes for a nice drive through the tunnels. Coming in V1.1... üêß 31 December - Version 1.1 Airport West added to the network as part of the Waterline extension , as an underground Waterline through station with 2 side platforms. Now shown in the intro , replacing Stepford Airport Central . New route: R014 2019 17 December - Version 1.4 Airport West is no longer shown in the intro , replaced by Northshore . 2022 12 June Sneak peek for Airport West's overhaul was released. After a bit of quiet while we have been working hard behind the scenes, here is the return of a series of #SneakPeekSundays! 27 August - Version 1.10 Station overhauled, new station building and is now located partially underground. OFF indicators added. Now an out-of-station interchange to Stepford Airport Parkway . Signal Zone moved from Zone F to Zone C . Added Waterline services to Newry Harbour , Airport Terminal 2 and the Esterfield branch . Route change: R014 ( Newry <> James Street ‚Üí Esterfield ) Now terminates at Esterfield. New routes: R016 , R017 & R018 Trivia [ ] The latest station model resembles the Charing Cross station in Glasgow. [ 1 ] The previous model resembled City Thameslink Station on the Thameslink network in London. This station and Cambridge Street Parkway used to be the only stations on Waterline with a travel time of 2 minutes between them. However, when V1.6 was released, there is also a timing of 2 minutes between Morganstown Docks and Morganstown . The rest only have 1 minute. As of V1.9 , more stations received a travel time of 2 minutes between them, such as Newry Harbour and Newry or between West Benton and Benton . This is the only Airport station not to be served by AirLink . Prior to V1.8 , Leighton City had a similar design to this station, primarily the platform walls. This was the only Waterline station to have had "Stepford" in its name, but "Stepford" was removed with the new human station announcements introduced in V1.8 . Despite this, the official station code from the V1.10 release notes for Airport West is still shown as "SAW". Similar to Airport Terminal 1 , 2 and 3 , which are "SAO", "SAX", and "SAZ" respectively, none of these stations include "Stepford" in their names. Prior to Version 1.10 : Only one route served this station, being R014 (then Newry <> James Street ) . The low ceilings on the platforms caused the top of the doors on some trains to reach above the ceiling. EMUs like the Class 379 and Class 730/0 had their pantographs going through the ceiling. After Leighton City 's upgrade in 1.8 , this was the only station to be fully underground. Despite being a station in the Airport Zone , there were no connections to any of the other airport stations, although one could walk to Airport Central to catch an AirLink train to the Airport Terminals. There was no connecting path between the stations. This station used to lack any OFF indicators despite being a dispatchable station, similar to Berrily . This station was located in signal Zone F as it is a Waterline station. This station had lifts, but ironically was not fully step free as there was a short escalator at the entrance to the ticket hall, which made it wheelchair accessible only for passengers who are inverse changing, and was also the last station on Waterline not having an entrance with wheelchair access. After Version 1.10 : The ceilings were raised with the upgrade of the station. The station was no longer fully underground, as there is an opening above the platforms. The station was moved near Stepford Airport Parkway , now located northwest of Stepford Airport Parkway, making the interchange the second OSI (out of station interchange) in the whole network. This station became a junction. Trains headed to Airport Terminal 2 branch off to the left, where as trains to Farleigh and Esterfield branch off to the right. There is an alphanumeric route indicator located on the signal before the junction, showing "A" for A irport Terminal 2 and "E" for E sterfield . This station was intended to be a terminal station, but the developers decided that the branch line for the station would be too short, so they added another station, James Street . The tracks between this station and James Street were the first lit up tunnels in the whole SCR system. The nearby Airport Terminal tunnels are also lit up. After leaving the station heading to Airport Terminal 2 , there is a Portal Access named " Hempstead Portal Access", a name nowhere mentioned in the game. Melrose Portal Access After leaving the station heading to James Street , there is a Portal Access named " Melrose Portal Access", a name nowhere mentioned in the game. The Waterline tracks between this station and James Street goes under Terminal 2 station. Hempstead Portal Access References [ ] ‚Üë Stepford Sunday | V1.10 is here! #010 (28 August 2022). Mattyx2013 on YouTube. Retrieved 30 August 2022. ## Station 5: Angel Pass

**Page ID:** 232
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Angel_Pass

**Summary:**
Angel Pass is a through station on the Stepford Main Line .

**Full Content:**

Angel Pass Overview Entrance 1 Entrance 2 Interior Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone AGP B Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) P1-3 Electrification Line Yes Stepford Main Line Station Information Location Stepford District Zone - Platforms 3 Tracks 4 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes & ticket office available Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station St Helens Bridge 0.6 mi / 1.0 km Bodin 0.4 mi / 0.6 km Angel Pass is a through station on the Stepford Main Line . It is served by limited Stepford Connect services to Stepford Central , Stepford Airport Central and Leighton City ; and Metro services to Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Barton , Port Benton and Morganstown . History [ ] 2017 30 December Angel Pass added to the network, located between St Helens Bridge and Bodin , as a Stepford Connect through station with 3 platforms, with Platform 2 & 3 being an island platform for services towards St Helens Bridge . Route changes: R001 , R002 & R003 Now stop here. 2018 6 December Sneak peek for a new passing track at Angel Pass was released, as part of Day 6 of the Advent Calendar. As of V1.1, two of our Connect routes will skip Angel Pass. To allow the network to flow freely for these express services we'll be introducing a passing track at Angel Pass. Here's a pic of it in action for Day 6! üèÇ 21 April - Version 1.0 Added Stepford Connect services to the Leighton Zone . New route: R004 Route change: R003 ( Stepford Central <> Winstree ‚Üí Leighton Stepford Road ) Now stops at Rocket Parade and terminates at Leighton Stepford Road . 31 December - Version 1.1 New passing track added towards Bodin . Added Stepford Connect services to Upper Staploe . Bodin P2-3 ‚Üí AGP P2, then P3 2023 3 March Sneak peek for Angel Pass' upgrade was released. It‚Äôs been a while hasn‚Äôt it! Well it‚Äôs time to get things back on track, so why not have a sneak peek! Coming very soon to an SCR branch near you! 6 March - Version 1.10.4 Station upgraded. Now resembles East Midlands Parkway station . Old second entrance is not demolished but is boarded up, with the new second entrance located to the left of it. There is still no option to spawn at the second entrance. 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 Angel Pass is now managed by Metro instead of Stepford Connect ; Stepford Connect services are once again limited. New routes: R132 , R133 , R134 , R135 , R136 & R137 Route removals: R024 , R025 , R033 & R045 No longer stop here. Trivia [ ] Since V1.10.4, the station resembles East Midlands Parkway station in Ratcliffe, though Angel Pass does not have a Platform 4 unlike the aforementioned station. This station has step-free access. There is a bypass track in the eastbound direction so that trains which are scheduled to skip this station can pass without being blocked by stopping trains. Similar layouts can be found at Elsemere Junction , Berrily , and Northshore . This is also the only station in the entire network to have a bypass track exclusive to Stepford Connect trains. The viaduct Stepford Express uses can be seen if the camera is zoomed out enough. Before the ex-cancellation of Metro , the viaduct was used by Stepford Connect services. In the past, this station was heavily criticised for being too blocky and old, with many members of the community calling for a complete overhaul of the station. The station was finally rebuilt in V1.10.4. With 1907 days of the station remaining basically the same, only minor upgrades were added overtime. These upgrades being a passing track, upgraded scenery and a new entrance. This station is rarely referred to as "AP" presumably to avoid confusion with A shlan P ark and Stepford A irport P arkway . Stepford Airport Parkway is thus commonly referred to as "SAP", with Angel Pass and Ashlan Park mostly referred to with their full names. When this station was originally released, it was not on the Network Map and onboard announcements were unavailable. This station was once the limited service station with the most number of services calling at it, until V1.8 when its limited service status was removed. With the upgrade in V1.10.4, the original secondary entrance was kept, which is boarded and has two signs that reads " This entrance is now closed, please use the new entrance to your left for access to Angel Pass station. Thank you. " There is also a rusted station sign in the bushes next to it. The second entrance was known for the largest station sign displayed in SCR, until it was removed in V1.10.4. It was very rare to see a train at Platform 3 as this station was typically not busy, however this changed in V1.8 , where trains were randomly allocated a platform, seeing more use of Platform 3. However in V1.10 , eastbound trains now prioritise Platform 2 again, as skipping at a multi-platform through station with random allocation caused SPADs . Signallers could not predict which platform a skipping train would enter, making it difficult to set the signal to proceed before the train reached it. Despite the management transfer to Metro in V2.2 , the station sign at the second entrance is still a Stepford Connect one. There used to be no direct connection to this station from Willowfield . Players would have to change at St Helens Bridge or Beechley instead. In V2.2 , R133 ( Willowfield <> Barton ) was added, connecting the two stations directly. ## Station 6: Ashlan Park

**Page ID:** 4755
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Ashlan_Park

**Summary:**
Ashlan Park is a through station on the Connolly Branch .

**Full Content:**

Ashlan Park Entrance Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Station Overview Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone APK F Station headcode Dispatching - No Electrification Line Yes Connolly Branch Station Information Location Benton District Zone - Platforms 2 Tracks 2 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines No Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station Cambridge Street Parkway 0.6 miles / 1.0 km Connolly 0.4 miles / 0.6 km Track Layout to Connolly to Cambridge Street Parkway Ashlan Park is a through station on the Connolly Branch . It is served by Waterline services to Newry Harbour , Newry , Benton and Connolly . This station was upgraded in Version 1.9.1, along with West Benton . To play these files, consider using another device or convert them into supported formats such as .mp3. History [ ] 2018 11 March Sneak peek for Ashlan Park was released. The more observant / nosey among you will have already seen this, but here is a picture of the stop just before Connolly, Ashlan Park 21 April - Version 1.0 Ashlan Park added to the network as part of the Connolly branch , as a Waterline through station with 2 staggered platforms. Based on Apperley Bridge station . New routes: R011 & R012 2022 25 May - Version 1.9.1 Station overhauled. Now based on Reston station . Removed staggered platforms for side platforms, as well as new scenery including a park. 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 Added OHLE. New route: R019 Trivia [ ] Prior to V1.9.1, Ashlan Park was based on Apperley Bridge station . After an overhaul in the aforementioned update, the station is based on Reston station . Before The Big Update was released, players could trespass to this station and Cambridge Street Parkway . The tracks from Cambridge Street Parkway ended here and they did not continue on to Connolly . There used to be a terminus branch leading from Platform 1 to 2 before its opening. Ashlan Park used to be the only station with staggered platforms across the whole Stepford County Railway network. However, in V1.8 , Woodhead Lane was overhauled and the station's platforms have been made staggered. As of V1.9.1, Ashlan Park have been overhauled without its staggered platforms. Interestingly, the revamped Ashlan Park looks like the pre- V1.8 Woodhead Lane , with a similar platform colour scheme and layout and a brown-ish bridge in the station. Pre- V1.8 Woodhead Lane Before V1.9.1, Ashlan Park heavily lacked scenery and there was nothing except road, bushes and the River Ben near the station, despite being called Ashlan 'Park'. This made Ashlan Park one of the most disliked stations in the game, and the most disliked station on Waterline , tied with the old Cambridge Street Parkway . The overhaul also connected the highway near Cambridge Street Parkway to Ashlan Park. Before the overhaul, it was just weirdly cut off before the tracks to Airport West . Strangely, the 6-lane motorway suddenly turns into a 2-lane level crossing with walking paths just before this station. This station, Beaulieu Park and Hemdon Park are the only stations in SCR to have "Park" in their names. If St Helens Park did open, it would be one of the only stations with "Park" in its name. This station has step-free access. Players can see the Benton Bridge , an ATC tower (probably the one at Stepford Airport) and the towers at Eden Quay if their render distance is high enough. A sneak peek released on the 18th April 2022 saw this station highly speculated to be overhauled in Version 1.9 . After the aforementioned update was released, it was later revealed to be Eden Quay . This station, along with West Benton 's overhaul, was not sneak peeked before V1.9.1's release. This is one of only five stations to have an elevator that serves more than two floors, the others being Stepford Central , Elsemere Junction , Stepford Airport Parkway and Rocket Parade . It is the only station not served by Stepford Connect and the only Waterline station with this trait. When!? 12 August - Version 2.0 Aslockby was added to the network as part of the Rayleigh Bay Branch , as a Stepford Connect through station with 2 staggered side platforms. New routes: R049 , R050 , R100 , R101 & R102 Trivia [ ] This station is the second station to have staggered platforms, the other being Woodhead Lane . This station has a rustic-style signal box similar to the Rayleigh Bay Signal Box and the Beaulieu Park Signal Box . However, this building is empty and non-functional. Despite this, it can still be accessed by Signallers . Platform 2 is not step-free due to there only being stair access via footbridge, making it one of the two stations to not be fully step-free along with Eden Quay . This station is one of the five Stepford Connect stations which do not have a route calling at Stepford Central , the others are Leighton West , Millcastle Racecourse , Carnalea Bridge , and Rayleigh Bay . It is possible to walk from Rayleigh Bay to this station. Notes [ ] ‚Üë Not in use Gallery [ ] A Class 156 at Aslockby, as seen in the V2.0 trailer. ## Station 8: Barton

**Page ID:** 24715
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Barton

**Summary:**
Barton is a terminus located on the Barton Branch that was added in Version 2.2 .

**Full Content:**

Barton Entrance Interior Platform View Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone BAR B Station headcode Dispatching B Yes (1 slot) P1-2 Electrification Line Yes Barton Branch Station Information Location Stepford District Platforms 2 Tracks 2 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates & card readers Service Information Preceding station Following station Coxly Newtown 0.2 mi / 0.3 km Elsemere Junction 0.6 mi / 1.0 km Barton is a terminus located on the Barton Branch that was added in Version 2.2 . It is served by Metro services to Willowfield , Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central & St Helens Bridge . This station forms the Barton Loop along with Coxly Newtown . To play these files, consider using another device or convert them into supported formats such as .mp3. History [ ] 2025 1 April - Version 2.1.3 A construction site was built to the right of Coxly . Metal beams at the construction site spelling out 'M' 'E' 'T' 'R' 'O' 11 May - Version 2.2 Barton added to the network as part of the new Metro operator, as a terminus of the Barton Loop. 'Closing the loop' by Sillysausage603 Trivia [ ] This station resembles Liverpool Central . This station is very close to Coxly Newtown at just 0.21 miles. This station is sometimes an overrun spot with trains coming up from Coxly Newtown as it comes up quick and around a corner. This station shares the "B" headcode with Benton . The other pairs of stations that share a headcode are Leighton Stepford Road and Rayleigh Bay , with "R", and Stepford Airport Parkway and Port Benton with "P". It is possible to walk from this station to Coxly & Berrily on road in a few minutes. Currently, station announcements that announce Barton contain an awkward pause before the station name is said. This station is one of the only stations where you don't need to turn around to start a new route, others being Port Benton and Leighton City . Currently the closest spawn point which can let drivers drive toward this station is the Beechley Sidings , which requires drivers to drive for about 15 minutes before arriving Barton. Due to this fact, when Version 2.2 was released, this station had relatively low traffic compared to the Metro Core Section due to traffic heading towards Barton having to pass through there. When Bodin TMD gets added in Version 2.3 , drivers will be able to spawn there and have access to a faster route to get to this station. ## Station 9: Beaulieu Park

**Page ID:** 4920
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Beaulieu_Park

**Summary:**
Beaulieu Park (pronounced as Byoo-lee Park ) is a through station that opened as part of Version 1.1 with the Stepford Connect extension to Morganstown . This station serves Metro services to Beechley , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge and Morganstown .

**Full Content:**

Beaulieu Park Entrance View Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Bird's Eye View Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone BPK B Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) P1-2 Electrification Line Yes Morganstown Branch Station Information Location Morganstown District Zone - Platforms 2 Tracks 2 Accessibility Level access & step-free access via lifts Ticket machines No Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station East Berrily 0.66 miles / 1.06 kilometres Morganstown 0.54 miles / 869 metres Preceding depot Following depot Berrily Depot - Track Layout to Morganstown Beaulieu Park Signal Box to East Berrily / Elsemere Junction Beaulieu Park (pronounced as Byoo-lee Park ) is a through station that opened as part of Version 1.1 with the Stepford Connect extension to Morganstown . This station serves Metro services to Beechley , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge and Morganstown . This station provides an out of station interchange with the nearby Whitney Green served and operated by Waterline . It received a major upgrade in Version 1.7 which revamped the station itself, the surrounding area, and the addition of Beaulieu Park Signal Box which controls Zone B, located next to the station. History [ ] 2018 13 December Sneak peek for Beaulieu Park was released, as part of Day 13 of the Advent Calendar. I hope you aren't tired of all the new stations yet! Day 13 brings you Beaulieu Park, a new station along the Connect extension ‚òÉÔ∏è Second upload for slightly better quality. 31 December - Version 1.1 Beaulieu Park added to the network as part of the Morganstown branch , as a Stepford Connect through station with 2 platforms for Stepford Connect and 2 platforms for AirLink . AirLink passes and does not stop here however. Provides out-of-station interchange to the nearby Whitney Green station. New route: R007 2020 22 June - Version 1.6 Added Stepford Connect services to the Willowfield branch . New route: R034 18 October Sneak peek for Beaulieu Park's overhaul was released. Yet another station to get a complete overhaul... Coming soon in SCR 1.7 29 October - Version 1.7 Station overhauled, AirLink and Stepford Express platforms removed. Platforms are now curved slightly, with a footbridge for access both platforms. Scenery near the station was upgraded. Beaulieu Park is now step-free. 2021 5 December - Version 1.8 Class 720 & Class 730/1 stop markers added to Platform 1 & 2. 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 Beaulieu Park is now managed by Metro instead of Stepford Connect ; Stepford Connect no longer serves this station. New routes: R130 & R131 Route removal: R007 No longer stops here. Trivia [ ] There is a station with the same name in Boreham, Essex. A video by video creator Geoff Marshall covering the station's construction site had a large amount of SCR players commenting on it, noting the identical name. This station is an out-of-station interchange between Metro and Waterline , due to the fact that players can walk to Whitney Green from the station. The most convenient way to get to Whitney Green is to follow the path to the park. Players can also walk to East Berrily from this station. Prior to V1.7 , this station was very bare. It contained two strange looking concealed stairwells, 2 bare platforms, some unused platforms on the AirLink tracks for no real reason, and really not much else. The area around it was also incredibly bland, with just some bushes and grass. Before its upgrade, this was one of the only stations in SCR to have neither CIS Boards nor Concourse Information Boards . Until their overhauls in V1.7 , this station looked very similar to East Berrily with its platform layout. However, East Berrily had a foot crossing unlike Beaulieu Park. This station, Ashlan Park and Hemdon Park are the only stations in SCR to have "park" in their name. This station used to be called " Beaulieu Park (Morganstown) ". However, when it opened, its name was shortened to just "Beaulieu Park". Before this station had been upgraded in V1.7 , this station's platforms were slightly shorter than the length of a 5-car train. When a 5-car train approached the station, the announcer would state that the doors of the rear coach would not open. This station's name is sometimes censored in the game chat for no reason. So the community calls Beaulieu Park by its initials: BP. However, "Beau lieu Park" does not get censored. There is a park near the station, however it is closer to Whitney Green than Beaulieu Park. The said park is also the spawn point for the aforementioned station. This station and East Berrily , are the only stations managed by Metro that are not joint managed by Transport for Stepford . The words "beau lieu" in French means "beautiful place", however, it is unknown whether or not the station's name is a coincidence. Notes [ ] ‚Üë This announcement was used in-game before the introduction of Metro , however, is no longer used. ## Station 10: Beechley

**Page ID:** 13368
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Beechley

**Summary:**
Beechley is a through station and a terminus on the Willowfield Branch . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Whitefield , Port Benton , Stepford Airport Central , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea ; and Metro services to Willowfield , Stepford Victoria , Stepford United Football Club , Barton , Berrily , and Morganstown .

**Full Content:**

Beechley Entrance Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Bird's Eye View Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone BCY A Station headcode Dispatching C Yes (1 slot) P1-4 Electrification Line Yes Willowfield Branch Station Information Location Stepford District Zone - Platforms 4 Tracks 4 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines None Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station Terminus Hemdon Park 1.54 miles / 2.48 kilometres Willowfield 2.74 miles / 4.41 kilometres City Hospital 0.33 miles / 0.53 kilometres Financial Quarter 0.73 miles / 1.17 kilometres Stepford Central 0.77 miles / 1.24 kilometres Preceding depot Following depot Willowfield Mainline Depot - Track Layout to Hemdon Park Beechley Sidings to City Hospital to Financial Quarter Beechley is a through station and a terminus on the Willowfield Branch . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Whitefield , Port Benton , Stepford Airport Central , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea ; and Metro services to Willowfield , Stepford Victoria , Stepford United Football Club , Barton , Berrily , and Morganstown . Opened in Version 1.6 , Beechley station is located at and serves the outskirts of Stepford City. It features 2 island platforms, Platform 3 and 4 for terminating services but is implied to be former through platforms due to the Beeching Axe. There is a siding right after this station, namely Beechley Sidings . It does not face Beechley, though. The Beechley Triangle is also located near Beechley, diverging to Stepford Victoria or Stepford Central . This station will be receiving a major overhaul in Version 2.3 . Proud to connect all of the diverse people and places of Stepford, including some new ones... üëÄ 22 June - Version 1.6 Beechley added to the network as part of the Willowfield extension , as a Stepford Connect through station and a terminus with 2 island platforms. New routes: R103 , R133 & R135 15 October - Sneak peek for Beechley's upgrade was released, based on Cardiff Queen Street station . The sun rising on a nice little revamp Coming to SCR version 2.3 üåá Trivia [ ] Beechley has not been upgraded since its release. The only change that has been made was the Metro rebranding in V2.2 . This station was previewed on 22 June 2020, and later opened on the same day as part of V1.6 . This was the only station on the Willowfield extension to be previewed to the community before its release. There is a nearby siding called Beechley Sidings . However, it does not lead to the station itself, and instead heads south to Stepford Central and Stepford Victoria . Beechley was City Hospital 's former name, but became its own station in V1.6 as the first stop along the Willowfield extension. The Willowfield extension was unknown to players, up until hours before the release of it. Before The Big Update , Beechley only existed on a map, as there was no station model built for it. The current Beechley is only around 600 metres away from City Hospital . Unused track beds are seen outside of the station. This is similar to many rail lines in the UK after The Beeching Axe in the 1960s. The word 'Beechley' used to be censored by Roblox's filtering, due to it containing the word 'beech', which sounds like a common vulgar word. 'Beachley', however, is fine. This trait is owned by Beaulieu Park , West Benton , Connolly , Coxly and Whitney Green , too. However, many other stations' names can be censored due to lag or chat restrictions. This is the only station along the entire Willowfield Branch to serve all services that use the branch, as some terminate here and do not carry on to Willowfield . This is one of only three stations to serve both routes to Stepford Victoria from the Willowfield branch, the other two being Financial Quarter and Stepford Victoria. Oddly, this station has no ticket machines. On the Stepford Connect map, the Morganstown Connect route shows its availability to go from Beechley to Morganstown. As of Version 2.2 , no Stepford Connect route exists that goes from Beechley to Morganstown nor to Berrily . R034 (now used for Metro ) used to originally be a Stepford Connect route, which follows the Morganstown Connect route lines. The same goes for R030 . Notes [ ] ‚Üë Not in use Gallery [ ] Prior to Version 2.2 [ ] Entrance Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Station Sign Other [ ] Sneak peek for Version 1.6 showcasing Beechley with a Class 68 and a Class 331/1 pride livery Sneak peek for Version 2.3 showcasing an upgraded Beechley with a Class 350 and a Class 756 Stations Willowfield ‚Ä¢ Hemdon Park ‚Ä¢ Beechley ‚Ä¢ Stepford Victoria ‚Ä¢ Financial Quarter ‚Ä¢ City Hospital ‚Ä¢ Stepford Central ‚Ä¢ Stepford East ‚Ä¢ Stepford High Street ‚Ä¢ Whitefield Lido ‚Ä¢ Stepford United Football Club ‚Ä¢ Woodhead Lane ‚Ä¢ Houghton Rake ‚Ä¢ Whitefield ‚Ä¢ St Helens Bridge ‚Ä¢ New Harrow ‚Ä¢ Elsemere Pond ‚Ä¢ Elsemere Junction ‚Ä¢ Berrily ‚Ä¢ East Berrily ‚Ä¢ Beaulieu Park ‚Ä¢ Morganstown ‚Ä¢ Angel Pass ‚Ä¢ Bodin ‚Ä¢ Coxly ‚Ä¢ Benton ‚Ä¢ Port Benton ‚Ä¢ Benton Bridge ‚Ä¢ Stepford Airport Parkway ‚Ä¢ Stepford Airport Central ‚Ä¢ Airport Terminal 2 ‚Ä¢ Hampton Hargate ‚Ä¢ Upper Staploe ‚Ä¢ Water Newton ‚Ä¢ Winstree ‚Ä¢ Rocket Parade ‚Ä¢ Leighton Stepford Road ‚Ä¢ Leighton City ‚Ä¢ Leighton West ‚Ä¢ Rayleigh Bay ‚Ä¢ Carnalea Bridge ‚Ä¢ Aslockby ‚Ä¢ Edgemead ‚Ä¢ Faymere ‚Ä¢ Westercoast ‚Ä¢ Millcastle Racecourse ‚Ä¢ Millcastle ‚Ä¢ Westwyvern ‚Ä¢ Starryloch ‚Ä¢ Northshore ‚Ä¢ Llyn-by-the-Sea Willowfield ‚Ä¢ Hemdon Park ‚Ä¢ Beechley ‚Ä¢ Stepford Victoria ‚Ä¢ Financial Quarter ‚Ä¢ City Hospital ‚Ä¢ Stepford Central ‚Ä¢ Four Ways ‚Ä¢ Stepford East ‚Ä¢ Stepford High Street ‚Ä¢ Whitefield Lido ‚Ä¢ Stepford United Football Club ‚Ä¢ St Helens Bridge ‚Ä¢ New Harrow ‚Ä¢ Elsemere Pond ‚Ä¢ Elsemere Junction ‚Ä¢ Berrily ‚Ä¢ East Berrily ‚Ä¢ Beaulieu Park ‚Ä¢ Angel Pass ‚Ä¢ Bodin ‚Ä¢ Coxly Newtown ‚Ä¢ Barton ‚Ä¢ Coxly ‚Ä¢ Benton ‚Ä¢ Port Benton ‚Ä¢ Morganstown Docks ‚Ä¢ Morganstown ‚Ä¢ Whitney Green ‚Ä¢ Upper Staploe List of Stations ‚Ä¢ List of Stations (Statistics) ‚Ä¢ List of Station Codes Upcoming stations are marked in italics , former stations are marked in strikethrough . ================================================================================

## Station 11: Benton

**Page ID:** 186
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Benton

**Summary:**
Benton is a major through station and terminus on the Stepford Main Line .

**Full Content:**

Benton Station Building Main Entrance North Entrance South Entrance Interior 1 Interior 2 Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Platform View 4 Platform View 5 Platform View 6 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone BEN F Station headcode Dispatching B Yes (3 slots) P8-13 , P4-7 , P1-3 Electrification Line Yes Stepford Main Line Station Information Location Benton District Zone Benton Zone Platforms 13 Tracks 14 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes & ticket office available Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Terminus (From CSP , BNB , PBN or MGT ) West Benton 0.5 mi / 0.8 km Coxly 1.1 mi / 1.8 km Eden Quay 1.6 mi / 2.6 km Newry 2.4 mi / 3.9 km St Helens Bridge 3.3 mi / 5.3 km Stepford Central 5.7 mi / 9.2 km Terminus (From SCN or SHB ) Cambridge Street Parkway 0.4 mi / 0.6 km Port Benton 0.5 mi / 0.8 km Benton Bridge 0.9 mi / 1.5 km Morganstown 1.0 mi / 1.6 km Hampton Hargate 1.4 miles / 2.3 km Leighton Stepford Road 5.7 mi / 9.2 km Preceding depot Following depot Coxly Bypass Siding Benton Siding Benton Depot Benton is a major through station and terminus on the Stepford Main Line . It is served by: Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Port Benton , Stepford Airport Central , Airport Terminal 2 , Leighton City , Leighton West , Edgemead , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea ; Metro services to Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Port Benton and Morganstown ; Waterline services to Newry Harbour , Newry , Connolly , Airport Terminal 2 , Farleigh , Esterfield , Morganstown and Greenslade ; Stepford Express services to Stepford Central , Newry Harbour , Newry , Leighton City and Llyn-by-the-Sea . Currently, this station serves as the hub for all Waterline services. The Benton Signal Box is located near the station, which controls Zone F. History [ ] 2017 25 November Benton added to the network, as a 3 (later 8) platform major through station to serve both Connect and WaterLine . New routes: R001 , R002 & R003 16 December Added Waterline services to Greenslade . New route: R013 20 December Added Waterline services to the Newry branch . New routes: R010 & Newry Harbour <> Greenslade 2018 21 April - Version 1.0 Added Stepford Connect services to the Leighton Zone . Added Waterline services to the Connolly branch . New routes: R004 , R011 & R012 Route change: R003 ( Stepford Central <> Winstree ‚Üí Leighton Stepford Road ) Now stops at Rocket Parade and terminates at Leighton Stepford Road. Route removal: Newry Harbour <> Greenslade Removed from the game. 31 December - Version 1.1 Added Stepford Connect services to the Stepford Victoria branch and Edgemead . Added Waterline services to the James Street branch . New routes: R005 , R006 , R009 & R014 Route change: R004 ( St Helens Bridge <> Leighton City ‚Üí Edgemead ) Now terminates at Edgemead. 2019 17 December - Version 1.4 Added Stepford Connect services to the Llyn-by-the-Sea branch. Added Stepford Express services to Stepford Central and the Llyn-by-the-Sea branch. New routes: R024 , R025 , R026 , R075 , R076 , R077 , R078 & R079 2020 22 June - Version 1.6 Added Stepford Connect services to the Willowfield branch . Added Waterline services to Morganstown . New routes: R015 , R032 , R033 , R035 & R036 7 October Sneak peek for Benton's overhaul was released. The biggest station transformation in the next update... We're really proud of this one - we hope you will be too! Coming soon in 1.7! 29 October - Version 1.7 Station overhauled, with the station now based on the new Birmingham New Street station . Platforms increased from 8 to 13. Platform 1-3 are for Waterline , with Platform 2 for terminating. Platform 4-6 & 11-13 are for Stepford Connect , with Platform 6 for terminating. Platform 7-10 are for Stepford Express , with Platform 8 & 9 for terminating. New route: R039 2021 5 December - Version 1.8 Platform allocation is now randomised at P1-3. Added Stepford Connect services to Upper Staploe and Leighton West . New route: R042 ( Benton <> Leighton West ) Route changes: R003 ( Stepford Central <> Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City ) R039 ( Benton <> Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City ) R076 ( Stepford Central <> Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City ) Now terminates at Leighton City. 2022 27 February - Version 1.8.2 New route: R045 15 May - Version 1.9 Added Stepford Express services to the Newry branch and services via Morganstown . New routes: R083 , R084 , R085 & R086 27 August - Version 1.10 Added Stepford Connect services to Airport Terminal 2 . Added Waterline services to Airport Terminal 2 and the Esterfield branch . New routes: R017 , R018 & R046 Route change: R014 ( Newry <> James Street ‚Üí Esterfield ) Now terminates at Esterfield. 2023 2 April - Version 1.10.7 New routes: R047 & R048 17 July - Version 1.10.8 HST & Class 80x stop markers added to Platform 1-3, 7 & 10. 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 New routes: R019 & R120 Version 2.0.1 Platform 8 extended and Platform 9 remodelled. Platform changes: Platform 2 now serves as a bi-directional overflow for Platform 1 & 3, still remains as the only terminating platform for Waterline / Stepford Express . Westbound platforms (P4-7) & eastbound platforms (P10-13) no longer limited by operator, now shared by both Stepford Connect & Stepford Express . Platform 8 is now an eastbound platform (for both CN & EX ), as well as a terminating platform with Platform 9 for Stepford Express from Stepford Central . Trains from Port Benton can now use Platform 12, with Platform 13 being no longer exclusive to trains from Port Benton. Trains from Benton TMD can only use Platform 11-13. 24 December - Version 2.1 New route: R088 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 Added Metro services. New route: R137 Trivia [ ] The old station resembled the old Birmingham New Street Station , located in Birmingham, UK . After the station's upgrade, the station now resembles the current Birmingham New Street Station . In real life, there is a station with the same name on the Tyne and Wear Metro . This station has step-free access. Benton has the second highest number of platforms out of all stations on the SCR network , at 13. It used to have lettered platforms which gave a total of 16 platforms, which meant it used to have the most platforms. The station with the most platforms is currently Stepford Central , which has 20 platforms. Benton was also the busiest station on the network until V1.1 , with all trains and routes stopping there, even from all depots. This used to be the second hub of Stepford Express (after Stepford Central ) before it was extended via Morganstown . It used to have more Stepford Express trains than Waterline trains because of it. As of V2.1 , 71% of Stepford Express routes stop here, tied with Leighton Stepford Road . [ note 1 ] As of V2.1 , this station serves the most amount of routes out of every other station on the SCR network, at 41 routes. Every Waterline route stops here. Benton only had three platforms when the game was originally released, but due to the number of routes that would run through the station, it was deemed not fit for that purpose, and the tracks were rerouted to a new station. The original entrance to the station no longer exists, and was replaced by the main entrance and the east concourse. The original station was later demolished and replaced. Until V1.7 , each platform entrance had signs for the destinations passengers could go to from each platform. These had not been updated between V1.0 and V1.6 and so were outdated and were later removed with the station overhaul. This is one of the first Waterline stations. Until Stepford Express was opened, in the old Benton, 4 platforms were unused, which gave this station the most unused platforms in all of SCR. All platforms have been in use since V1.4 and after the station's upgrade. A walking route is provided from Benton to West Benton and even further down the line towards Stepford and Newry . There used to be a walking route between here and Port Benton , but after the station upgrade, the road and the pathways were removed for an unknown reason. This station is one of 7 stations on the SCR network which were operated by Network Rail . This station was not wheelchair accessible before being revamped in V1.7 . This is the only station in the game with terminating-only tracks in both directions. The speed limit between here and West Benton used to be 75 MPH, but it was lowered to 45 MPH from West Benton in V1.4.1 and to West Benton in V1.6 . This station received a major renovation in V1.7 . This renovation removed 3 platforms (or added 5 platforms, depending on how the platforms are counted before the renovation) and brought more of a splash of colour and design. The old platforms were numbered 1A, 1B, 2A, 2B, 3, 4A, 4B, 5A, 5B, 5C, 6A, 6B, 7A, 7B, 8A and 8B. Before the aforementioned update, this station had the most amount of lettered platforms in the game, at 15. These platforms were removed and replaced by numerical platforms 1-13. The upgrade also removed the East Concourse entrance, which was the last place players could see the old "rectangle" style ticket barriers. When coming in from the Main Entrance, players will be able to see "the eye" of Birmingham New Street station , the station Benton is based on. They can also see the shopping centre up above. This station is one of five multi-line through stations that are always stopped at by every route that approaches it, with the others being Newry , Stepford Central and Stepford Airport Central . Prior to the station overhaul in V1.7 , players could buy SUFC merch from a stand right outside the station. If a player is driving R039 ( from Leighton City ) and R044 ( from Leighton West ) and attempts to bypass Platforms 6 eastbound, the driver will be despawned with the message "Don't eat the buffers!", despite there not being any buffers at the end of the platform. The track after Platform 2 splits into two, with one track heading to West Benton and the other going into Benton Siding (and from West Benton ). This is likely for the return to depot feature. Strangely, there is an unused through track located between Platform 3 and 4. This track links the end of Platform 3 to the track after Platforms 4-7. This is probably used for freight trains between Airport Parkway and Newry Harbour . A series of electric boxes was added in V1.9 , between Coxly and Benton. However, little players noticed it as it was barely noticeable when driving at full speed. Players can walk from here all way to Stepford without trespassing. If players decide to walk from Stepford to Benton, it would take approximately 18-20 minutes to arrive at their destination. Players can access the roof of this station. This is possible by jumping on commercial buildings located on the second floor. Benton is named after the river Ben . This station shares the headcode "B" with Barton . The only other pairs of stations that share a headcode are Port Benton and Stepford Airport Parkway , which both share the "P" headcode and Leighton Stepford Road and Rayleigh Bay , which both share the "R" headcode. This station has a total of 131 stop marker signs. ## Station 12: Benton Bridge (Station)

**Page ID:** 190
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Benton_Bridge_(Station)

**Summary:**
Benton Bridge is a through station on the Stepford Main Line , with services continuing to Hampton Hargate or the Airport Branch .

**Full Content:**

This page is about the Stepford Connect station. For the bridge, see Benton Bridge (Structure) . Benton Bridge Entrance Interior Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Bridge Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone BNB C Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) P1-4 Electrification Line No Stepford Main Line Station Information Location Benton District Zone Benton Zone Platforms 4 Tracks 4 Accessibility Step-free access via ramps Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gate Service Information Preceding station Following station Benton 0.9 mi / 1.5 km Stepford Airport Parkway 0.7 mi / 1.1 km Hampton Hargate 0.7 mi / 1.1 km Benton Bridge is a through station on the Stepford Main Line , with services continuing to Hampton Hargate or the Airport Branch . It serves Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Benton , Stepford Airport Central , Airport Terminal 2 , Leighton City , Leighton West , Edgemead , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea . The station received an overhaul in Version 1.7 and will be receiving another overhaul in Version 2.3 . History [ ] 2017 25 November Benton Bridge added to the network, as a Stepford Connect through station with 2 side platforms. New route: R001 29 November New route: R003 19 December Station was upgraded. 2018 21 April - Version 1.0 Added Stepford Connect services to the Leighton Zone . Route changes: R003 ( Stepford Town <> Winstree ‚Üí Leighton Stepford Road ) Now stops at Rocket Parade and terminates at Leighton Stepford Road. New route: R004 31 December - Version 1.1 Benton Bridge is now dispatchable. Added Stepford Connect services to Stepford Victoria . Route change: R004 ( St Helens Bridge <> Leighton City ‚Üí Edgemead ) Now terminates at Edgemead. New route: R005 2019 17 December - Version 1.4 Added Stepford Connect services to the Llyn-by-the-Sea branch. New routes: R024 & R025 2020 22 June - Version 1.6 Added Stepford Connect services to the Willowfield branch . New route: R035 28 August Sneak peek for Benton Bridge's overhaul was released. Another station with a bit of an upgrade! All coming soon in the next big SCR update :D 29 October - Version 1.7 Station overhauled, now has 2 island platforms (4 platforms). Services to and from Stepford Airport use Platform 1 & 4; and services from Benton and Hampton Hargate use Platform 2 & 3. Added Stepford Connect services to Upper Staploe . New routes: R009 & R044 2022 27 February - Version 1.8.2 New route: R045 27 August - Version 1.10 Added Stepford Connect services to Airport Terminal 2 . New route: R046 2023 2 April - Version 1.10.7 New route: R048 2025 2 November Sneak peek for Benton Bridge's upgrade was released, based on Brent Cross West station . The old infrastructure is water under the bridge around here! üåâ Coming to SCR version 2.3 Trivia [ ] The frontage of this station is based on Didcot Parkway station . In Version 2.3 , it will be based on Brent Cross West station . This station has step-free access, though there is no lift access. This is because the paths towards the platforms are ramps, not stairs. At the western end of the platform is the River Ben and at the eastern end is the interchange of tracks going to and from Stepford Airport Parkway and Hampton Hargate . Before V1.1 , Benton Bridge was not a dispatchable station. Prior to V1.8 , R009 , and the two Class 68 exclusive routes R026 and R036 were not scheduled to stop at this station. However in V1.8 , R009 was changed to stop here. A lot of people on the Discord server thought this station should be remodeled to decrease traffic. It was remodeled, although is still sometimes a bottleneck, especially heading east towards Stepford Airport Central and Leighton / Llyn . This station used to have the only 2 car stop on Stepford Connect , specifically for the Class 158 /9. Prior to the upgrade, some old signs could be found on the footbridge of this station. The sign for platform 1 said "This platform for trains to to Stepford Central via Coxly " and the sign for platform 2 said "Trains to Stepford Airport and Leighton ". The signs don't mention St Helens Bridge , Stepford Victoria , Edgemead , Westwyvern , Llyn-by-the-Sea , Beechley and Willowfield . These signs and the entire footbridge were removed when the station was completely rebuilt in V1.7 . Prior to V1.7 , this station only had 2 platforms. On the 28th of August 2020, Charlie_RBX sneak peeked an upgraded Benton Bridge saying "Another station with a bit of an upgrade! All coming soon in the next big SCR update". In the sneak peek, there are new commercial buildings, including one named "The Daily Sausage", as a reference to the newspaper in Mind the Gap. On the following day (29 August 2020), a sneak peek of Benton Bridge (the structure) was posted, showing that the bridge has been upgraded into a large suspension bridge, scenery updates around Port Benton , electrification on the Morganstown bridge and several static ships in the surrounding waters. However, some people criticised the new bridge, saying that the gradient of the bridge is too steep for trains and therefore not realistic. Platform 1 allows trains bound for Stepford Airport Central to load without causing traffic for trains towards Hampton Hargate , vice versa. Stepford bound trains can use both Platform 3 and Platform 4 at the same time, although there is only one westbound Stepford Connect track on Benton Bridge (Structure) , so trains have to wait for each other to pass. Though trains from Hampton Hargate cannot go on Platform 4 and trains from Stepford Airport Parkway cannot go on Platform 3. Despite the station lacking electrification, EMU units are still able to serve the station. The same issue also applies to Morganstown Docks . ## Station 13: Berrily

**Page ID:** 4882
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Berrily

**Summary:**
Berrily is a through station and terminus that opened as part of Version 1.1 along the Stepford Connect extension to Morganstown .

**Full Content:**

Berrily Entrance Interior 1 Interior 2 Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Terminating Platform View Operational Information Served by Managed by (Eastbound only) Station code Signal zone BRY B Station headcode Dispatching Y Yes (1 slot) P1-4 Electrification Line Yes Morganstown Branch Station Information Location Stepford District Zone - Platforms 4 Tracks 6 Accessibility Step-free access via lift Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Elsemere Junction 0.6 mi / 1.0 km St Helens Bridge 2.3 mi / 3.7 km (From SHB only) Terminus East Berrily 0.5 mi / 0.8 km Morganstown 1.9 mi / 3.1 km Stepford Airport Parkway 2.5 mi / 4.0 km (Eastbound only) Berrily is a through station and terminus that opened as part of Version 1.1 along the Stepford Connect extension to Morganstown . This station provides Stepford Connect services to Stepford Central and Morganstown ; Metro services to Willowfield , Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge and Morganstown ; and limited AirLink services to Stepford Airport Central . The AirLink route ( R054 ) that stops at this station is for Airport-bound trains only, and all Stepford-bound services skip on the mainline track without a platform. History [ ] 2018 8 December Sneak peek for Berrily was released, as part of Day 8 of the Advent Calendar. We didn't just extend Connect to Stepford Victoria... we've actually split off at St Helens Bridge for another Connect extension. Say hello to Berrily, part of your expanded Connect network... ‚õ∑ 31 December - Version 1.1 Berrily added to the network as part of the Morganstown branch , as a Stepford Connect through station and terminus with limited AirLink services to Stepford Airport Central only. Resembles Kentish Town station 's Thameslink platforms. New routes: R007 , R008 & R054 2020 15 April - Version 1.4.6 ( Ten Million Update ) New route: R027 22 June - Version 1.6 Platforms and scenery near Berrily was upgraded. Added Stepford Connect services to the Willowfield branch . New route: R030 , R034 29 October - Version 1.7 Station entrance and concourse upgraded. Removed the Metro red. 2021 5 December - Version 1.8 Lift access added, Berrily is now step-free. 2023 17 July - Version 1.10.8 Class 80x stop marker added to Platform 4. 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 Berrily is now managed by Metro instead of Stepford Connect ; Stepford Connect no longer terminates here. Added Metro services. New routes: R130 & R131 Trivia [ ] This station bears resemblance to Kentish Town station , specifically the Thameslink platforms. It is also said it resembles West Ealing station . When this station opened, despite being quite a large station, it did not have CIS boards . The same could be said for Morganstown prior to V1.4.1 . There is no platform for AirLink trains going to Stepford Central . To get to this station from the Airport, passengers should take an AirLink service to Morganstown , then change for Stepford Connect or Metro services. It is believed that Berrily has a thriving berry-growing industry, due to its name being a direct nod to the word "berry", and the fact that there is a berry company near the station ( Berry's Berries of Berrily ). The announcements for this station and New Harrow used to glitch and break the station's announcements. This was fixed in V1.3.29. This is AirLink 's least used station as only a single route on their network, R054 , stops at Berrily. Also, due to the absence of a platform for westbound services to Stepford Central , westbound R054 services do not stop at this station. Ironically, the AirLink HQ is located near this station. Walking accessibility is present to Elsemere Junction with the road running alongside the many commercial buildings . This station has two unused tracks alongside with its platforms. This station, although served by Stepford Connect and AirLink , had Metro red colours, as this station was formerly proposed for Metro . This was changed in V1.7 . The same could be said for both Stepford High Street and Whitefield before V1.4.1 . This station, despite being dispatchable, had no OFF indicators. This was also the case with Airport West and Cambridge Street Parkway . This station received a minor scenery update in V1.6 , with the platforms and buildings near the station being renovated. The game's Origin Point (0,0,0) is located here. This was referenced in the 50-million-visit scavenger hunt in V1.10.1 . In V1.7 , the entrance and concourse of Berrily got a revamp, although the platforms themselves remained mostly the same. This station has a footbridge with lifts, although the station was not step-free before V1.8 , because the concourse and the platforms were only connected through a short staircase. This made it step-free for interchange only, similar to Airport West and Stepford Airport Parkway . In V1.8 , a lift was added near the concourse. Since then, this station has full step-free access. There is a depot located near this station. This station could be named after former Product Developer yrrebRBLX, who is named Alex Berry in real life. This station is known in the community for being content creator Dweller 's 'loved' station. He later revealed that his love for the station was purely for satire. As shown in the AirLink operator map , Berrily is shown to be bi-directional unlike Airport Terminal 1 (meaning there are services towards Stepford Central ), though this may just be an oversight. Many players have also hoped to have a westbound platform at this station, though this may never be added as Berrily is unique for only having an eastbound platform for AirLink , otherwise it would just be similar to Elsemere Junction . This is the only station that is owned by Metro that AirLink stops at. Prior to Version 2.2 , it was one of the two Stepford Connect owned stations that are served by AirLink , the other being Water Newton . In 2022, a youtuber called Dweller made a joke about this station saying "Berrily is a pog", because of how many people skipped, or overshoot it. But a youtuber called Trainspotting Mayhem made a diss track called "Trainspotting Mayhem - Berrily Ain't Pog (Berrily diss track)". . The joke has been closed ever since. Notes [ ] ‚Üë Not in use Gallery [ ] Prior to Version 1.7 [ ] Entrance Concourse Prior to Version 2.2 [ ] Entrance Interior 1 Interior 2 Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Terminating Platform View ## Station 15: Bodin

**Page ID:** 197
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Bodin

**Summary:**
Bodin is a through station on the Stepford Main Line .

**Full Content:**

Bodin Spawn Entrance Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone BOD B Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) P1-3 Electrification Line Yes Stepford Main Line Station Information Location Stepford District Zone - Platforms 3 Tracks 5 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Angel Pass 0.4 mi / 0.6 km St Helens Bridge 1.0 mi / 1.6 km Coxly 1.2 mi / 1.9 km Coxly Newtown 1.0 mi / 1.6 km Bodin is a through station on the Stepford Main Line . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Port Benton , Stepford Airport Central , Airport Terminal 2 , Leighton City , Edgemead , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea ; and Metro services to Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Barton , Port Benton and Morganstown . Bodin is a medium sized suburb with apartments to the right side of Bodin station. VisitBodin is its promotional campaign founded by former Community Director Thehazad9 (now Product Developer ) to boost visits to this area.
