History [ ] 2017 25 November Bodin added to the network, as a Stepford Connect through station with 5 platforms. Platform 1 & 2 is for eastbound services, while Platform 3 is for westbound services. Platform 4 & 5 contain no tracks and is unused. New routes: R001 , R002 & R003 30 November Footbridge added to the station. 2018 21 April - Version 1.0 Station overhauled, along with the addition of Bodin TrainCare next to the station. Platform layout changed to 3 side platforms, with 2 passing tracks between them. Platform 2 is now for westbound services. Bodin is no longer dispatchable. Added Stepford Connect services to the Leighton Zone . New route: R004 Route change: R003 ( Stepford Central <> Winstree ‚Üí Leighton Stepford Road ) Now stops at Rocket Parade and terminates at Leighton Stepford Road . 31 December - Version 1.1 Added Stepford Connect services to the Stepford Victoria branch and Edgemead . New routes: R005 , R006 & R009 Route change: R004 ( St Helens Bridge <> Leighton City ‚Üí Edgemead ) Now terminates at Edgemead. 2019 16 September - Version 1.3.26 ( Five Million Update ) Bodin is now shown in the intro , replacing Stepford East . 17 December - Version 1.4 Bodin is no longer shown in the intro , replaced by Llyn-by-the-Sea . Added Stepford Connect services to the Llyn-by-the-Sea branch. New routes: R024 , R025 & R026 2020 22 June - Version 1.6 Now joint managed with Transport for Stepford . Added Stepford Connect services to the Willowfield branch . New routes: R032 , R033 , R035 & R036 6 September Sneak peek for Bodin's overhaul was released. Sneak peeked Bodin overhaul 29 October - Version 1.7 Station overhauled, now resembles a scaled down Reading station with 3 platforms. Track layout remains the same. Bodin is now dispatchable again. 2021 5 December - Version 1.8 Platform allocation is now randomised at P2-3. Added Stepford Connect services to Upper Staploe . Route changes: R003 ( Stepford Central <> Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City ) Now stops at Upper Staploe and terminates at Leighton City. Announcement change: The Stepford Connect announcement is now: https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:BodinC.ogg instead of: https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:BodinC_1.7.mp3 2022 27 February - Version 1.8.2 New route: R045 27 August - Version 1.10 Added Stepford Connect services to Airport Terminal 2 . New route: R046 2023 2 April - Version 1.10.7 New routes: R047 & R048 2024 12 September - Version 2.0.1 OHLE is now meshed. 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 Bodin is now managed by Metro instead of Stepford Connect . New routes: R132 , R133 , R134 , R135 , R136 & R137 Trivia [ ] The station's design resembles a very scaled down Reading station in real life. A gold statue of Thehazad9 is located next to this station. Climbing on top of the statue, grants the badge "Mayor of Bodin". The plaque used to be outdated prior to V1.6 , for it stated that Thehazad9 was the Chief Operations Officer (now called Operations Director ). He was the Community Director (then called People Director ) after this before resigning in October 2019. The old plaque could be found in the bushes near the tracks towards Stepford. This station was next to Bodin TrainCare . Bodin Depot was nearby, but it was demolished in The Big Update . Bodin TrainCare was removed in V1.7 . This was the only station to have more than 2 platforms with no island platforms. According to the sneak peek, the upgraded Bodin has one side platform and one island platform, with passing tracks of Stepford Express between the side platform and island platform. It also has an upgraded footbridge with the word "BODIN" on top of it. This station was one of three stations shown in the Stepford County Railway Intro because of the Class 755 /3 (which is in a special 5 million visits livery) being displayed at Bodin TrainCare , replacing Stepford East in the Five Million Update . It was then replaced by Llyn-by-the-Sea in V1.4 . The other two stations featured in the intro are Rocket Parade (BanTech's HQ) and Airport West (which was replaced by Northshore ). Before Version 1.7 , this was one of only 4 stations with old Banner Repeaters, along with St Helens Bridge , Angel Pass and Morganstown . However, this station was not dispatchable before the aforementioned version. There were once CD/RA indicators here, however, very few people ever got the chance to use them before they were removed. CD/RA dispatching is a proposed feature on the roadmap, so they could be added back soon. This station has become infamous after Charlie_RBX's account was incorrectly terminated on the 24th June 2020, due to a Roblox moderator incorrectly flagging the new announcement for "Bodin" as an inappropriate word, and caused his account to be briefly terminated for a few hours due to an "inappropriate username". In the bushes next to the statue, there was once a rusty sign which used to be on the statue, as Thehazad9 was the People Director (later renamed to Relations Director and Community Director ) before he became Product Developer , which then made the sign incorrect. The sign was changed in V1.6 adding this extra ‚Äúeaster egg‚Äù, but as Thehazad9 has since became Relations Director (later renamed to Community Director ) again, the sign became inaccurate. In V1.7 , when the station got upgraded, the sign was again updated, however, he resigned down to PDV again, making the sign once again inaccurate. The sign can now be found laid next to the Stepford City bound tracks before the station. In V1.8 , the train announcements for "Bodin" changed and is slightly different to the V1.7 version. This also happened with Water Newton . The main difference in the current version is that the 'O' is said with more emphasis. In 2020, Bodin was awarded "Capital of Culture" by the fictional committee of the same name. After fraudulently claiming the status was extended to 2022, Bodin was disqualified for the status in 2021 and banned from consideration in 2022. This was explained in an apology from the committee found in advertisements around the SCR Network. Oddly, fewer Metro routes serve this station than Stepford Connect , yet Metro manages this station instead of Stepford Connect as of V2.2 . ## Station 16: Cambridge Street Parkway

**Page ID:** 447
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Cambridge_Street_Parkway

**Summary:**
Cambridge Street Parkway is a through station located on the Connolly and Esterfield Branches .

**Full Content:**

Cambridge Street Parkway Entrance Interior Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Footbridge Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone CSP F Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) P1-3 Electrification Line Yes Connolly Branch Esterfield Branch Station Information Location Benton District Zone - Platforms 3 Tracks 3 Accessibility Step-free access via ramp Ticket machines Yes & ticket office available Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Benton 0.4 mi / 0.6 km Ashlan Park 0.6 miles / 1.0 km Airport West 0.9 mi / 1.5 km Track Layout to Ashlan Park / Airport West to Benton Cambridge Street Parkway is a through station located on the Connolly and Esterfield Branches . It is served by Waterline services to Newry Harbour , Newry , Benton , Connolly , Airport Terminal 2 , Farleigh and Esterfield . History [ ] 2018 21 April - Version 1.0 Cambridge Street Parkway added to the network as part of the Connolly branch , as a Waterline through station with 4 platforms. Based on Cambridge North station . New routes: R011 , R012 & R014 2019 7 August - Version 1.3.21 Cambridge Street Parkway is now dispatchable. 2021 23 October Sneak peek for Cambridge Street Parkway was released. Sneak peeked Cambridge Street Parkway overhaul 5 December - Version 1.8 Station overhauled, platforms decreased from 4 to 3. Now based on M3 Parkway station . Platforms are no longer specific to whether the train heads to Ashlan Park or Airport West . 2022 27 August - Version 1.10 Added Waterline services to Airport Terminal 2 and the Esterfield branch . Route change: R014 ( Newry <> James Street ‚Üí Esterfield ) Now terminates at Esterfield. New routes: R016 , R017 & R018 2023 31 August - Version 1.10.9 Banner repeater has been added at Platform 3 to improve visibility. 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 Added OHLE. New route: R019 Trivia [ ] Prior to V1.8 , Cambridge Street Parkway was based on Cambridge North station . With its overhaul in V1.8, this station's building now takes the basis of M3 Parkway station in Ireland. This station became slightly busier after the James Street Branch (now Esterfield Branch) was added in Version 1.1 . In V1.10 , its usage has increased again, with three new routes stopping at the station. [ 1 ] Before V1.1 , it was the only Waterline station that had platforms not in use. The station became dispatchable in V1.3.21, although few ever dispatched there due to players rarely driving Waterline . This station and Stepford Airport Parkway are the only parkway stations in SCR. Cambridge Street Parkway and Airport West used to be the only stations on Waterline with a travel time of 2 minutes between them, but when the Morganstown Shuttle was released, Morganstown Docks and Morganstown also have a time of 2 minutes between them. The rest only have <1 minute. Though in V1.9 , timings between Waterline stations have increased due to complaints and the Newry branch upgrade. The station's name on the old driver HUD prior to V1.10 Cambridge Street Parkway has the second longest station name in-game at 24 characters, with the longest being Stepford United Football Club with 29, and the third longest being Leighton Stepford Road with 22. Prior to V2.0 , the name of this station is so long that on the Driver HUD, 'Parkway' is cut off. After V2.0 , the driver HUD now shows the full name of the station. Prior to its removal in V1.8 , there was a sign in the ticket hall says "Frequent services to Benton from Platforms 2 and 4". Ironically, few drivers ever drove Waterline services, and even fewer drove services stopping at this station. From V1.8 to V1.9 , this station had the most parking spaces, at 234. However, Stepford Airport Parkway has beaten this record with its upgrade in V1.10 with a total of 1,013 spaces. Station rebuild posted on 23 October 2021 Prior to V1.8 , many players heavily criticized the station due to the bare colour scheme and lack of scenery nearby, and hoped that there would be an improvement or rebuild of the station in future. Eventually, former Managing Director Charlie_RBX previewed this station rebuilt on the 23rd of October 2021, evident of the station sign. This station was then upgraded in V1.8 . The billboard in the background is a reference to rock band Oasis . After the station's overhaul in V1.8 , access to the platform was replaced with ramps instead of stairs, making this station having step-free access. Prior to V1.8 , this station had two platforms each for eastbound and westbound services (1 & 3 for Eastbound, 2 & 4 for Westbound). Platform 1 and 2 was for services to and from Connolly , and Platform 3 and 4 for services to and from James Street . After the overhaul in V1.8 , Platform 4 was demolished. Platform 3 was converted into a westbound platform, leaving only 1 platform for eastbound services. There are also no longer separate platforms for services to Connolly and services via Airport West . The abandoned structure of Platform 4 and its track beds can still be seen in the station. ## Station 17: Carnalea Bridge

**Page ID:** 23055
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Carnalea_Bridge

**Summary:**
Carnalea Bridge is a bi-directional through station on the Rayleigh Bay Branch .

**Full Content:**

Carnalea Bridge Entrance Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone CLB H Station headcode Dispatching - No Electrification Line No Rayleigh Bay Branch Station Information Location Leighton District Zone - Platforms 1 Tracks 1 Accessibility Step-free access via ramps Ticket machines No Ticketing None Service Information Preceding station Following station Rayleigh Bay 0.52 miles / 0.84 kilometres Aslockby 0.60 miles / 0.97 kilometres Track Layout to Aslockby Carnalea Bridge Sidings (Decorative only) to Rayleigh Bay Carnalea Bridge is a bi-directional through station on the Rayleigh Bay Branch . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Leighton City , Leighton West , Rayleigh Bay , Edgemead , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea . It was added along with Aslockby and Rayleigh Bay in Version 2.0 . Contents 1 Station layout 1.1 Legend 1.2 Legend 2 Services 3 Station announcements 4 History 5 Trivia 6 Notes Station layout [ ] Stopping Passing G Platform Exit Platform 1 ‚Üê Stepford Connect to Rayleigh Bay ( RLB ) ‚Üí Stepford Connect to Leighton City , Leighton West , Edgemead , Westwyvern & Llyn-by-the-Sea ( ALB ) Legend ‚Üê Eastbound ‚Üí Westbound G Platform Exit Platform 1 ‚Üê Stepford Express to Rayleigh Bay ( RLB ) ‚Üí Stepford Express to Llyn-by-the-Sea ( EDG ) Legend ‚Üê Eastbound ‚Üí Westbound Services [ ] Platform(s) Previous station Route Next station 1 Rayleigh Bay R049 to Edgemead Aslockby R050 to Llyn-by-the-Sea R100 to Leighton West R101 to Leighton City R102 to Westwyvern Aslockby R049 R050 R100 R101 R102 to Rayleigh Bay Rayleigh Bay Station announcements [ ] Type Audio Platform https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:CLBP.ogg https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:CLBC.ogg N/A N/A https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:CLBE.ogg [ note 1 ] Please note: iOS and iPadOS do not natively support playing .ogg audio files and will show an error. To play these files, consider using another device or convert them into supported formats such as .mp3. History [ ] 2024 27 July Sneak peek for Carnalea Bridge was released. We're on one track towards version 2.0 12 August - Version 2.0 Carnalea Bridge added to the network as part of the Rayleigh Bay branch , as a Stepford Connect through station with 1 bi-directional platform. New routes: R049 , R050 , R100 , R101 & R102 Trivia [ ] This station resembles Galashiels station in Scotland. As of Version 2.0 , this station is one of the three single platform stations on the network, the others being Leighton West and Airport Terminal 1 . This station is the only station out of the three to be bi-directional, as well as being the only station to be completely bi-directional on the network. This is the only station on the entire network to not have any signals on or near its platform. Given that there are no signals near this station, the signalling desk cameras barely show the platform. As there are no nearby signals, OFF indicators or banner repeaters, Guards can immediately blow their whistles and close the doors when the train finishes loading, without needing to check the signal aspect. This station is one of the five Stepford Connect stations which do not have a route calling at Stepford Central , the others are Leighton West , Millcastle Racecourse , Aslockby , and Rayleigh Bay . Although named " Carnalea Bridge ", the closest bridge is only a small one near Rayleigh Bay . ## Station 18: City Hospital

**Page ID:** 4712
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/City_Hospital

**Summary:**
City Hospital is an elevated through station located at the end of the Stepford Victoria and Willowfield Branches.

**Full Content:**

City Hospital Entrance Concourse Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Bird's Eye View Bird's Eye View with NHS buildings Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone CHP A Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) P1-2 Electrification Line Yes Willowfield Branch Stepford Victoria Branch Station Information Location Stepford District Zone Stepford City Zone Platforms 2 Tracks 2 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Beechley 0.4 miles / 0.6 km Financial Quarter 0.4 mi / 0.6 km Stepford Victoria 0.7 mi / 1.1 km Stepford Central 0.4 mi / 0.6 km Preceding depot Following depot - Beechley Sidings Track Layout to Beechley to Financial Quarter to Stepford Central City Hospital is an elevated through station located at the end of the Stepford Victoria and Willowfield Branches. It is served by limited Stepford Connect services to Stepford Victoria and Airport Terminal 2 ; and Metro services to Willowfield , Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford United Football Club , Berrily , Morganstown , Barton and Port Benton . This station serves the nearby Stepford City Hospital . Trivia [ ] This station has step-free access, however, there is only 1 lift in this station, which is strange considering that there is a hospital nearby. The Willowfield Branch separates from the Stepford Victoria Branch west of this station. There is an actual hospital near this station called Stepford City Hospital (formerly called Stepford General Hospital ) This station was originally going to be called Beechley . The name has since been used by a new station that opened in V1.6 . The "NHS" buildings When seen from above, the buildings near the station spell out the acronym "NHS", which is the National Health Service of the United Kingdom. This was added in 2020, to show support of the National Health Service during the COVID-19 Pandemic. There is a train station with the same name in Northern Ireland. This station was originally a part of the Metro Loop but since the cancellation of Metro , it was instead reopened in V1.1 as a part of the Stepford Victoria Branch . The lights in the concourse of the station are in different colours, those being red, orange, yellow and green in that order. ## Station 19: Connolly

**Page ID:** 4748
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Connolly

**Summary:**
Connolly is the terminus of the Connolly Branch , located on the banks of the River Ben .

**Full Content:**

It is served by Waterline services to Newry Harbour , Newry and Benton . Feel like y'all deserve an update for your patience! Here is a sneak peEk at the new Connolly station building! (a few more pics to come below, hang tight a sec!) 21 April - Version 1.0 Connolly added to the network as part of the Connolly branch , as a Waterline terminus with 3 platforms with a siding in the middle. New routes: R011 & R012 31 December - Version 1.1 Connolly is now dispatchable. 2020 22 June - Version 1.6 Station headcode: C ‚Üí O C was taken by Beechley . 2021 5 December - Version 1.8 Scenery overhauled. Siding now has a not-in-service Class 730/0 . Random platform allocation added. 18 December - Version 1.8.1 Fix : Parked Class 730/0 no longer displays "Welcome on board Stepford Connect " on its PIS . 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 Added OHLE. New route: R019 Trivia [ ] The station is based off of King's Lynn station in real life. There is a real-life station with the same name in Dublin, Ireland. This station has step-free access. This station was built by AMAviation, a former Control Centre Manager . It was very rare for a train to terminate on Platform 2 or 3 here, because there are rarely two or more trains at Connolly at the same time, since not many drivers drive Waterline . This was changed in V1.8 as platform allocation is changed to be random and trains have an equal chance to enter either 3 platforms. Before The Big Update , the Connolly extension was visible from the refurbished Benton station but services could not run on it. This station is named after Louie Connolly (DauntlessRBLX), a former Manager and contributor to Stepford County Railway . There is a track with no platform surrounding it between the tracks for Platform 1 and 2. After V1.8 , it was occupied by a not-in-service Class 730/0 . Before the station opened, it was supposed to be called Rose Dale Head . This was referenced from an old sign at Newry . Similar to Beechley and Willowfield , its name was later partially reused for Rosedale Village in V1.10 . This is the northernmost point the River Ben can be seen. Just south of this station is a tributary, which is a small stream. Players are able to see Eden Quay from here if their render distance is high enough. Many players like this station due to its good scenery compared to other stations nearby like Ashlan Park and James Street prior to their refurbishments. This station's name is censored in game chat for no reason. In order to get around the restrictions, Connolly has been said in different ways, including: Connoly, Conolly or Conno. This happens to Berrily , Beaulieu Park , Upper Staploe , West Benton and Whitney Green , too. Beechley is also censored, but it has a reason after all. Many other stations' names can be censored due to lag or because of safe chat. This is one of the three stations to have a train stabled directly next to/in the station, the other two being Whitefield and Esterfield . Part of the roof and pillars of the station, as well as the information boards still have the old Waterline colours. Gallery [ ] Scenery around the station before V1.8 Station Entrance with the old WaterLine signage. ## Station 20: Coxly

**Page ID:** 188
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Coxly

**Summary:**
Coxly is a through station on the Stepford Main Line .

**Full Content:**

Coxly Entrance Interior View 1 Interior View 2 Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone COX B Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) P1-3 Electrification Line Yes Stepford Main Line Station Information Location Stepford District Zone - Platforms 3 Tracks 5 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Bodin 1.18 miles / 1.9 kilometres Benton 1.04 miles / 1.67 kilometres Coxly is a through station on the Stepford Main Line . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Port Benton , Stepford Airport Central , Airport Terminal 2 , Leighton City , Edgemead , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea ; and Metro services to Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Port Benton and Morganstown . Coxly Sidings is located adjacent to this station, with a bypass siding and a station siding . These replaced the former Coxly Depot , which was also located near this station. This station was overhauled in Version 1.6 and Version 1.10 . History [ ] 2017 25 November Coxly added to the network, as a Stepford Connect through station with 5 platforms. With express tracks between (7 tracks total). Platform 1-3 is for eastbound services, while Platform 4-5 is for westbound services. New routes: R001 , R002 & R003 2018 21 April - Version 1.0 Added Stepford Connect services to the Leighton Zone . New route: R004 Route change: R003 ( Stepford Central <> Winstree ‚Üí Leighton Stepford Road ) Now stops at Rocket Parade and terminates at Leighton Stepford Road . 31 December - Version 1.1 Added Stepford Connect services to the Stepford Victoria branch and Edgemead . New routes: R005 , R006 & R009 Route change: R004 ( St Helens Bridge <> Leighton City ‚Üí Edgemead ) Now terminates at Edgemead. 2019 17 December - Version 1.4 Added Stepford Connect services to the Llyn-by-the-Sea branch. New routes: R024 , R025 & R026 2020 25 May Sneak peek for Coxly's overhaul was released. Sneak peeked Coxly overhaul along with the Class 68 22 June - Version 1.6 Station overhauled, platforms reduced from 5 to 3. Platform 1 & 2 is for eastbound services, while Platform 3 is for westbound services; Platform 1 is also the platform for trains from Coxly Station Siding . Now joint managed with Transport for Stepford . Added Stepford Connect services to the Willowfield branch . New routes: R032 , R033 , R035 & R036 2021 5 December - Version 1.8 Platform allocation is now randomised at P1-3. Added Stepford Connect services to Upper Staploe . Route changes: R003 ( Stepford Central <> Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City ) Now stops at Upper Staploe and terminates at Leighton City. 2022 27 February - Version 1.8.2 New route: R045 27 August - Version 1.10 Station upgraded, with the station building and platform canopies receiving a new design. Platform layout remains the same. Platform priorities added, allocation is no longer randomised. Bodin P1 ‚Üí Coxly P2, then P1 Added Stepford Connect services to Airport Terminal 2 . New route: R046 2023 2 April - Version 1.10.7 New routes: R047 & R048 2024 12 September - Version 2.0.1 OHLE is now meshed. 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 Coxly is now managed by Metro instead of Stepford Connect . The footbridge has been upgraded. New route: R137 Trivia [ ] The station's platforms resemble a scaled down Denmark Hill station in south London. Before V1.6 , at the top windows which could be seen from trains heading towards Benton , they were once home to the old signalling room , which was left empty before its removal. The one in use currently is the Stepford ROC . Before the refurbishment of Coxly in V1.6 , players could still see its entrance, which was located at the front end of Platform 1 behind the signal. However, no one could enter anymore as it was completely locked up. There were two other entrances to the signalling room in the past, which were located at the station concourse and on Platform 2, but they were removed after its closure. The Old ROC & Coxly Layout. There are two passing tracks between Platforms 2 and 3 which are used by Stepford Express . When Coxly Depot was in operation, drivers from the Stepford City Zone often have their TPWS systems kick in and activate the emergency brakes due to trains from the depot passing in front of them, and the signal system does not give way to trains on the main line first. Formerly, Dispatcher Trainings were held here. Dispatcher trainings have also been held at Stepford United Football Club , Faymere and Willowfield in the past. New players often overshoot this station from both Bodin and Benton as the speed limit on either side of the station is increased to 100 MPH and the players oftentimes do not pay attention to how close their next stop is. SPADs also frequently happen at the eastbound platforms towards Benton as drivers spawning from Coxly Station Siding pass the signal on accident, as it is not located at the end of the platform. Players can walk from here to Stepford and Benton without trespassing. Oddly, fewer Metro routes serve this station than Stepford Connect , yet Metro manages this station instead of Stepford Connect as of V2.2 . ## Station 21: Coxly Newtown

**Page ID:** 7430
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Coxly_Newtown

**Summary:**
Coxly Newtown is a through station on the Barton Branch .

**Full Content:**

Coxly Newtown North Entrance South Entrance North Ent. Tunnel Concourse Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone CXN B Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) P1-2 Electrification Line Yes Barton Branch Station Information Location Stepford District Platforms 2 Tracks 2 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts at south entrance Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Bodin 1.0 mi / 1.6 km Barton 0.2 mi / 0.3 km Coxly Newtown is a through station on the Barton Branch . It is served by Metro services to Beechley , Stepford Victoria and Barton . From Version 1.6 to Version 2.1.5 , this station was closed down. Players could get to the station's entrances without trespassing, but the entrances and its platform were sealed with metal plates. Construction of the station began in Version 2.1.3, and the station opened in Version 2.2 . This station forms the Barton Loop along with Barton . The Transport for Stepford headquarters is located near this station, opposite of the south entrance. History [ ] 2017 25 November Plans for an operator under the name " Metro " were first created as a rapid rail transit system. 2018 21 April - Version 1.0 Plans for Metro were scrapped and the station was left abandoned. 2020 22 June - Version 1.6 Entrances have been sealed up by metal plates. 2025 1 April - Version 2.1.3 Station construction began with construction barriers surrounding both entrances. 11 May - Version 2.2 Coxly Newtown added to the network as part of the new Metro operator, as a through station on the Barton branch . New routes: R132 , R133 , R134 , R135 & R136 5 August - Version 2.2.1 A poster named "5 minutes earlier" was added at Platform 1. This won the first Community Spotlight hosted in May 2025. '5 minutes earlier' by Ourodeprata Trivia [ ] This station resembles Conway Park station . Along with Robinson Way and Upper Staploe (Metro) , this is one of only three stations remaining from the legacy plans. Additionally, Coxly Newtown is the only operational station of the three. The Transport for Stepford headquarters is located opposite to the south entrance of this station. The north entrance is the only remaining evidence of the original Coxly Newtown. Before the modern planning of Metro , the trains were planned to go to Coxly Newtown, then straight into Coxly , where they either terminate or continue onto the mainline. According to the SCR Hub Site , this is the least used station in the game, although this may be due to its recent reopening compared to other older stations in-game. ## Station 22: East Berrily

**Page ID:** 4929
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/East_Berrily

**Summary:**
East Berrily is a through station that opened as part of Version 1.1 for the Stepford Connect extension to Morganstown . It is served by Metro services to Beechley , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge and Morganstown . This station received a major upgrade in Version 1.7 .

**Full Content:**

History [ ] 2018 21 December Sneak peek for East Berrily was released, as part of Day 21 of the Advent Calendar. Coming towards the end of the list of new stations that will be available in V1.1... Day 21 reveals East Berrily station üåü 31 December - Version 1.1 East Berrily added to the network as part of the Morganstown branch , as a Stepford Connect through station with 2 platforms for Stepford Connect and 2 platforms for AirLink , AirLink passes and does not stop here however. New route: R007 2020 22 June - Version 1.6 Added Stepford Connect services to the Willowfield branch . New route: R034 20 September Sneak peek for East Berrily's overhaul was released. Yet another station to receive an overhaul in the next update... Haven't the builders been busy?! Coming soon to an SCR near you 29 October - Version 1.7 Station overhauled, AirLink and Stepford Express platforms removed. Now resembles Ashfield station . Scenery near the station was upgraded. 2021 5 December - Version 1.8 East Berrily is now dispatchable. Route removal: R034 ( Beechley <> Morganstown ) No longer stops here. 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 East Berrily is now managed by Metro instead of Stepford Connect ; Stepford Connect no longer serves this station. New routes: R034 , R130 & R131 Route removal: R007 No longer stops here. Trivia [ ] The latest station model resembles Ashfield station in Glasgow. Prior to the overhaul, the level crossing at this station originally despawned people who walked on it. This was fixed, and players can now cross without penalty. In Version 1.7 , the foot crossing was removed and replaced with a foot/road bridge. Until their overhauls in Version 1.7 , this station looked very similar to Beaulieu Park with its platform layout. However, Beaulieu Park did not have a foot crossing then. Players can walk from this station to Beaulieu Park . Players can walk to Berrily Depot from this station, but the road cuts off just before reaching Berrily . There was a commercial building called "Greenslade Security" next to this station. In Version 1.7 it was moved and now sits on top of the tracks beyond the station. In the sneak peek released on 20 September 2020, the AirLink tracks were not present. People at the time speculated that AirLink / Stepford Express services would pass on East Berrily's platforms, or they would run on tracks that were not seen in the sneak peek. It was not known that the slow tracks slightly diverge off the mainline to serve this station. The scenery blocks the fast tracks from view. This also happened with the Upper Staploe sneak peek. Before Version 1.7 , the stretch between Berrily , East Berrily, and Beaulieu Park was very under detailed and lacking in scenery, with just one road and bushes. After the update, the whole Morganstown branch became very detailed, arguably as detailed as the Stepford City Zone . Because this station has short platforms, the rear doors on 5/6 coach trains do not open. This also happens in Hemdon Park , Woodhead Lane , New Harrow and Elsemere Pond . Beaulieu Park used to have this trait. However, its platform is now long enough for some 5 coach trains to fit after the upgrade in Version 1.7 . This station became dispatchable in Version 1.8 . Alongside Beaulieu Park , this station is one of the 2 stations managed by Metro that aren't joint managed by Transport for Stepford . Notes [ ] ‚Üë This announcement was used in-game before the introduction of Metro , however, is no longer used. ## Station 23: Eden Quay

**Page ID:** 5127
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Eden_Quay

**Summary:**
Eden Quay is a through station located on the Newry Branch . It is served by Waterline services to Newry Harbour , Newry , Connolly , Airport Terminal 2 , Farleigh , Esterfield , Morganstown and Greenslade ; and limited Stepford Express services to Newry and Leighton City .

**Full Content:**

New routes: R010 & Newry Harbour <> Greenslade 2018 14 March Sneak peek for Eden Quay's scenery overhaul was released. SNEAK PEEK I am very pleased to show you the new Eden Quay area! The station had no exit nor scenery so we did something about it! 21 April - Version 1.0 Station scenery overhauled, is now elevated above a river, with the iconic Eden Quay buildings added nearby. Station structure remained the same overall. Added Waterline services to the Connolly branch . New routes: R011 & R012 Route removal: Newry Harbour <> Greenslade Removed from the game. 31 December - Version 1.1 Added Waterline services to the James Street branch . New route: R014 2021 5 December - Version 1.8 Announcement change: The Waterline announcement is now: https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:EdenQuayW.ogg instead of: https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:EdenQuayC.ogg 2022 18 April Sneak peek for Eden Quay's overhaul was released. The first of the next series of sneak peeks coming to you in the near future. Something feels different, but what could it be? Coming Soon 15 May - Version 1.9 Station overhauled, is no longer above water but is still near a river. Scenery upgrades around the station, with the iconic Eden Quay buildings moved further away from the station however. Added limited Stepford Express services to Newry and Leighton City . New route: R086 27 August - Version 1.10 Added Waterline services to Airport Terminal 2 and the Esterfield branch . Route change: R014 ( Newry <> James Street ‚Üí Esterfield ) Now terminates at Esterfield. New routes: R017 & R018 2023 17 July - Version 1.10.8 Class 80x stop markers added to Platform 1 & 2. 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 New route: R120 Trivia [ ] The newest station model is based on Dockyard station in Devonport, Plymouth, England. Prior to The Big Update , there was no water beneath the station, and no buildings surrounding it. It was on the grass surrounded by bushes, with no exit and no scenery. Before Version 1.9 : This was one of the few stations in the game that did not have a road near their entrance. The other stations with this trait are Stepford Airport Central , Airport Terminal 1 , Airport Terminal 2 , and Airport Terminal 3 . This was the only overground station on the entire SCR network that did not have a direct, ground-level entrance. Airport Terminal 1 also has this trait, however it is situated underground. This was the only station to be completely above water (even the entrances). This was the only station to have a tilted station sign. This was the only elevated station on Waterline . The station was not dispatchable. This was the only station in SCR that was built on a quay/river. Financial Quarter does not count because it is only above a river and not built on a river. In other words, it is not entirely on water If the player goes around the harbour, they will come across a foot crossing. This station has step-free access, but for Platform 2 only, as there is a short staircase at the entrance to Platform 1. Hence, passengers requiring step-free access will have to take a northbound train to Newry for inverse changing if they wish to travel southbound from this station. As of V1.9 , this is the only Stepford Express station which is not fully step-free. As of V2.0 , this station and Aslockby are the only stations which are not fully step-free. Members of the SCR Community often call this station in a parodical name - "Eden Quack". Eden Quay is somewhat an "icon" station for Waterline , due to the number of Waterline adverts featuring this station and the scenic view of the lights on the buildings, especially at night. There is an underpass to the south of the station entrances, which you can walk under. This station can be difficult for Dispatchers as the only way to switch platforms is by exiting the station, walking across a bridge, and then re-entering the station. This may cause slight delays for trains. This is the only Stepford Express station where the short platform announcement can be heard on the Class 221 and Class 800 , which only the front 4 coaches fit into the station. There is a quay with the same name in Ireland. **Page ID:** 2003

Edgemead is a through station and a bi-directional terminus on the Stepford Main Line served by Stepford Connect and Stepford Express .

**Full Content:**

Is that another fresh lick of paint I see? ü§î Coming very soon to an SCR near you! 19 February - Version 1.7.2 Station overhauled, new station building and platforms and a Concourse Information Board added. Now based on Fareham station . Platform 1 is now a through platform; Platform 2 is now a bi-directional terminating platform, which allows the new R040 to terminate from Llyn-by-the-Sea . New route: R040 5 December - Version 1.8 Signal Zone moved from Zone D to Zone E . Added Stepford Connect services to Leighton West . Route changes: R037 ( Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City <> Llyn-by-the-Sea ) R038 ( Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City <> Westwyvern ) Now terminate at Leighton City. New routes: R041 & R042 2023 17 July - Version 1.10.8 Class 80x stop markers added at Platform 1 & 3. 2 November - Version 1.10.10 Bug : Trains from the Leighton City / Leighton West direction cannot terminate. 2024 30 January Sneak peek for Edgemead's second overhaul was released. What a refreshing feel this sunrise brings 12 August - Version 2.0 Station overhauled, now based on Newark Northgate station . Platform 1 now also serves terminating services, with Platform 2 serving through services. Added Stepford Connect & Stepford Express services to the Rayleigh Bay branch . New routes: R049 , R050 , R100 , R101 , R102 & R087 Bugfix : Trains can now terminate from the Leighton City/West direction again. 24 December - Version 2.1 New route: R088 Trivia [ ] The station is based on Newark Northgate station in Nottinghamshire, England. Previously, it was based on Fareham station in Hampshire, England. This station, along with Rayleigh Bay and Westercoast , are the only stations served by Stepford Express that are managed by Stepford Connect . Some longer-standing members of the community affectionately call the barn outside of Edgemead, towards Leighton City "Mugmead" after former SSG Muggenzifter . The station name Edgemead is a compound word of "edge" and "mead" (meaning a meadow), likely referring to its location away from Leighton and how it is located in a more countrysided area. However, due to "mead" also meaning a type of alcohol, the name is sometimes censored in the in-game chat, leading to players calling the station joke names like "Edgemeat" or "Eggmeat". This station, along with Leighton Stepford Road , Leighton City , and Leighton West , are 4 consecutive terminating stations with no through stations in between. The old Platform 1 used to be rarely used after V1.4 as most players drove beyond Edgemead towards Llyn-by-the-Sea , and it could only be used by R004 and R009 which terminate at Edgemead. This is one of the two stations where trains from both directions can terminate at the same platform, the other being Leighton City . This station is the third station to use the turnaround mid-route functionality, after Airport Terminal 2 and 3 . At the north of Edgemead, a rusty post for the banner repeaters of signal S383 and S385 can be seen which held the banner repeaters for the signals before Platform 1 and 2. ## Station 25: Elsemere Junction

**Page ID:** 4923
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Elsemere_Junction

**Summary:**
Elsemere Junction is a through station on the Morganstown Branch that was added in Version 1.1 .

**Full Content:**

History [ ] 2018 17 December Sneak peek for Elsemere Junction was released, as part of Day 17 of the Advent Calendar. I'm running out of ways to introduce a new station, but for Day 17, have another one... ü•Ç 31 December - Version 1.1 Elsemere Junction added to the network as part of the Morganstown branch , as a Stepford Connect through station with 4 platforms with a passing track for AirLink trains. New routes: R007 , R008 & R053 2019 1 February - Version 1.1.9 Added AirLink services to Airport Terminal 1 & 2 . Added limited Stepford Express services to Stepford Central / Westwyvern . New route: R082 2021 26 September Sneak peek for Elsemere Junction's overhaul was released. And the next station overhaul‚Ä¶ Coming soon to v1.8! 5 December - Version 1.8 Station overhauled, new station building and platforms are more detailed. Now resembles Worcestershire Parkway station . New routes: R130 , R131 , R132 , R133 , R134 , R135 & R136 Trivia [ ] The current version of this station resembles Worcestershire Parkway station . This station only has one passing track instead of two for both directions. The same goes for Angel Pass and Northshore . This may cause SPADs to occur when an AirLink or Stepford Express train is loading at Platform 3 and there is a train that skips this station behind it, as the speed limit is increased to 125 MPH before this station. Numerous commercial buildings make up some of the scenery near this station, including the famous PizzabyBilly. Currently, this is the only AirLink station joint managed with Transport for Stepford . This is currently the only station that is managed by AirLink but not located in the area of the former Airport Zone . This is also currently the only station served by Stepford Express and Metro that is managed by AirLink . Despite being an AirLink station, only two routes ( R053 and R059 ) service at the station, meaning it is considered a limited station on the AirLink map. Like Leighton Stepford Road , this station used to owned by Connect before V1.6 Currently, only one Stepford Express service ( R082 ) stops here. This station and Eden Quay are the only Stepford Express served stations that do not receive direct services to Llyn-by-the-Sea . Prior to V1.8 , even though Stepford Express serves this station, it was not available on their operator spawn options. If players wanted to spawn as a Passenger or a Guard at this station, they needed to use the AirLink or Stepford Connect list. This issue has now been fixed. This station has walking access to Berrily via a road placed on the side of several commercial buildings . This station and Elsemere Pond are the second closest stations on the network, with a distance of 0.26 miles between each other. The line between Port Benton and Morganstown Docks beats this by 0.09 miles with a distance of 0.17 miles apart. As a result, announcements do not say the stations the train will be calling at between these two stations because of the short distance. This station is one of the 6 triple-line junctions alongside Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Benton , Airport Terminal 2 and Leighton Stepford Road . This is the only station on the Morganstown branch that was not overhauled in V1.7 . When the sneak peek for the overhaul in V1.8 was released, some have incorrectly speculated that the passing track will be removed for AirLink / Stepford Express trains to Stepford Central , as it is not seen in the image and appears to be facing Stepford City . This is because the sneak peek was facing the concourse which was on the west side at that time. However, this remained unconfirmed as the image is facing the direction towards Morganstown , not Stepford Central , with evidence of Signal A025 and the platform number. Ultimately, the passing track remained in V1.8 and the concourse has been moved to the eastern side of the station. Before V1.8 , this station was not dispatchable despite having OFF indicators. Elsemere Junction is unique for featuring platform deck detailing; this can also be seen at Financial Quarter . When the station announcer announces services for R082 ( Stepford Central <> Westwyvern via Morganstown ), the train announcer still says " Stepford Express , service to: Westwyvern , via, Morganstown ." even though Elsemere Junction is already on the Morganstown Branch . Until V2.2 with the opening of the Barton Loop , this station wasn't actually a junction despite having had the name "Junction" in it. ## Station 26: Elsemere Pond

**Page ID:** 5125
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Elsemere_Pond

**Summary:**
Elsemere Pond is a through station on the Morganstown Branch . It is served by Metro services to Willowfield , Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Berrily , Morganstown and Barton .

**Full Content:**

History [ ] 2018 20 December Sneak peek for Elsemere Pond was released, as part of Day 20 of the Advent Calendar. Day 20 brings you Elsemere Pond üéÜ 31 December - Version 1.1 Elsemere Pond added to the network as part of the Morganstown branch , as a limited-service Stepford Connect through station with 2 platforms. New route: R008 2020 15 April - Version 1.4.6 ( Ten Million Update ) New route: R027 22 June - Version 1.6 Added Stepford Connect services to the Willowfield branch . New route: R030 29 October - Version 1.7 Station and scenery overhauled, with a footbridge added. 2023 6 March - Version 1.10.4 Elsemere Pond is now part of the training map. 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 Elsemere Pond is now managed by Metro instead of Stepford Connect ; Stepford Connect no longer serves this station. Station overhauled, resembles Ainsdale station . New routes: R034 , R130 , R131 , R132 , R133 , R134 , R135 & R136 Trivia [ ] Currently, this station resembles Ainsdale station . This station has step-free access. The eastbound platform is accessible via a ramp at the entrance and the westbound platform can be accessed either via the footbridge or foot crossing. Passengers needing step-free access to the westbound platform should use the foot/road crossing. All Metro services call at this station, with Stepford Connect no longer stopping at the station. In V1.7 , the station's position on the map changed. This station gets its name from the pond nearby and the area where it is located. This station was one of the few stations in the game where players can only cross platforms by crossings. A footbridge has been added in V1.7 . Until V1.1.3, the foot crossing was broken as kill blocks were left in. It is possible to walk from here to New Harrow and Angel Pass without trespassing. It is possible to walk to St Helens Bridge via a road running alongside the railway tracks. This station and Elsemere Junction are the second closest stations on the network, with a distance of 0.26 miles apart. However, the line between Port Benton and Morganstown Docks beats this by just 0.09 miles with a distance of 0.17 miles between each other. The foot/road crossing here is a popular place to stand and get flung by passing AirLink and Stepford Express services which often pass through at speed when not slowing to stop at Elsemere Junction . The station is immediately after the viaduct for Stepford Express services via Morganstown and merge onto the AirLink tracks. No Stepford Express or AirLink services stop here though as no platforms exist. In the training map introduced in Version 1.10.4, Elsemere Pond is one of two through stations. Elsemere Pond did not recieve direct services to Morganstown until the addition of Metro in V2.2 . Notes [ ] ‚Üë This announcement was used in-game before the introduction of Metro , however, is no longer used. ## Station 27: Esterfield

**Page ID:** 19897
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Esterfield

**Summary:**
Esterfield is a terminus on the Esterfield Branch .

**Full Content:**

Esterfield Entrance Interior Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone EFD G Station headcode Dispatching Q Yes (1 slot) P1-4B Electrification Line Yes Esterfield Branch Station Information Location Farleigh District Zone - Platforms 5 (4 in use) Tracks 4 Accessibility Level access Ticket machines Yes & ticket office available Ticketing Ticket gates & card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station Farleigh 2.1 mi / 3.4 km Rosedale Village 1.1 mi / 1.8 km Terminus Preceding depot Following depot - Esterfield Mainline Depot Esterfield is a terminus on the Esterfield Branch . It is served by Waterline services to Newry and Benton . This station was released along with Farleigh and Rosedale Village as part of the Waterline Extension in Version 1.10 . Esterfield TMD is located next to this station. Contents 1 Station layout 1.1 Legend 1.2 Exits 2 Services 3 Station announcements 4 History 5 Trivia 6 Gallery 7 Notes Station layout [ ] G Platforms ‚ä£ Waterline terminating platform ‚Üê Waterline to Newry & Benton ( RDV / FAR ) ‚î§ Concourse & waiting area [ Exit 1 ] Platform 1 Island bay platform Platform 2 ‚ä£ Waterline terminating platform ‚Üê Waterline to Newry & Benton ( RDV / FAR ) ‚î§ ‚ä£ Waterline terminating platform ‚Üê Waterline to Newry & Benton ( RDV / FAR ) ‚î§ Platform 3 Island bay platform Path [ Exit 2 ] Platform 4B Platform 4A ‚ä£ Waterline terminating platform ‚Üê Waterline to Newry & Benton ( RDV / FAR ) Parked Class 143 ‚î§ Legend [ ] ‚Üê Eastbound ‚ä£ Terminal ‚î§ Buffer Exits [ ] ‚Üë Main exit ‚Üë Car park exit Services [ ] Platform(s) Previous station Route Next station 1-4B Terminus R014 to Newry Farleigh R016 to Benton Rosedale Village Station announcements [ ] Type Audio Platform https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:EsterfieldP.ogg https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:EsterfieldC.ogg https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:EsterfieldM.ogg https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:EsterfieldW.ogg https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:EsterfieldE.ogg Please note: iOS and iPadOS do not natively support playing .ogg audio files and will show an error. To play these files, consider using another device or convert them into supported formats such as .mp3. History [ ] 2022 24 July Sneak peek for Esterfield was released. Bringing you the worst, best kept secret in the whole of Stepford county... 27 August - Version 1.10 Esterfield added to the network as part of the Waterline extension , as a 4 platform Waterline terminus. Based on Clacton-on-Sea station . Platform 4 is a split platform with Platform 4A and 4B, Platform 4A is unused however. New routes: R014 & R016 Trivia [ ] Esterfield is heavily based on Clacton-on-Sea station in Essex. This station is one of the two stations to have split platforms, the other being Morganstown . However, Platform 4A is not used, and has a Class 143 parked in it. Benton shared this trait before V1.7 ; Newry also shared this trait before V1.9 . This station was highly anticipated by the community, as the name was leaked over a year before its official opening, evident of leaked audio files containing the name that were found as early as 2021. The name of this station was inspired by an older project by BanTech , under his old account Jelly134. His first popular game, Esterfield Bus Simulator (EBS) was a UK based bus simulator that existed around 2012. While this game is no longer available to play, permission from BanTech has been acquired to re-publish some version of the game on the catalog. The shunt signal at platform 4B does not stop trains from passing it. This makes players approaching Platform 4B able to pass the shunt signal and crash into the Class 143 parked at platform 4A. If a player attempts to hit the Class 143 however, they will get despawned with the "Don't eat the buffers!" message although there are no buffers after Platform 4B. Sometimes a driver can crash into the parked Class 143 if the driver is laggy and enters the platform at full speed. This station, along with Airport Terminal 2 [ note 1 ] , has the most platforms served by Waterline trains than any other station, with four. This station also has the most platforms out of any station owned by Waterline , with five. Esterfield (Q), as well as Farleigh (J), Leighton West (K), Airport Terminal 2 (X) and Airport Terminal 3 (Z), do not have a letter in their name that is their station headcode . The station has a parked E200 MMC outside the main station entrance, however the bus is for scenery only. Just outside the station, there is a playground with a roundabout, a swingset, a slide, and tables. However, the slide and the roundabout has no collisions. There is a church next to the playground with a cemetery. Gallery [ ] Sneak peek of Esterfield, published by Community Director tjh44 on 24 July 2022 A Class 143 parked at Platform 4A A Class 143 terminating at Platform 4B Esterfield station at night Station sign as seen in game Notes [ ] ‚Üë Airport Terminal 2 mainly serves AirLink trains. However, due to platform allocations being randomised, Waterline trains can terminate on any platform. Hence, Waterline trains can use all four platforms at the station. New routes: R011 & R012 Route removal: Newry Harbour <> Greenslade Removed from the game. 1 December Sneak peek for Faraday Road's overhaul was released, as part of Day 1 of the Advent Calendar. Day 1... üéÖ your first sneak peek of version 1.1: 31 December - Version 1.1 Station overhauled. Platforms increased from 2 to 3. Platform 3 leads to nowhere however. Added Waterline services to the James Street branch . New route: R014 2019 13 June - Version 1.3.13 Platform 3 is now in use, for ECS trains from Faraday Road Depot towards Newry . 2021 5 December - Version 1.8 Faraday Road is now dispatchable. Announcement change: The Waterline announcement is now: https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:FaradayRoadW.ogg instead of: https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:FRC.ogg 2022 15 May - Version 1.9 Scenery near Faraday Road was upgraded. Track and platform layout remains unchanged. Stepford Express services can now pass this station. 27 August - Version 1.10 Added Waterline services to Airport Terminal 2 and the Esterfield branch . New routes: R017 & R018 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 New route: R120 12 September - Version 2.0.1 Platform 3 can now serve as a bypass/overflow to Platform 2. ECS trains from Faraday Road TMD can still only use Platform 3. Trivia [ ] Faraday Road loosely resembles Stetchford station . This station has step-free access. This station's renovation was the first item on the V1.1 Advent Calendar. In V1.1 , this station received a major upgrade as voted for by hundreds on the SCR Discord server. It is possible to hear traffic from the mainline a half mile down. Prior to V2.0.1, Platform 3 used to be only for ECS trains coming out of Faraday Road TMD . Unlike Platform 1 at Coxly , where there is a similar station layout, there was no crossover track for mainline trains to enter Platform 3. Prior to V1.0 , Eden Quay was designed to similar specifications to this station. The Class 730/0 in the sidings used to say "Welcome on board Stepford Connect " despite belonging to Waterline . This was patched in V1.10 . The Waterline Headquarters is located right next to this station. The depot shown in the Driver menu when picking a train is actually floating above near this station. In order to see it, players would need a high render distance and graphics and looked above Faraday Road Depot . However, this was fixed in a later update where the depot would turn invisible for players not in the menu. Stepford Express trains do not stop at this station, including R086 that is able to spawn at Faraday Road TMD . ## Station 29: Farleigh

**Page ID:** 19894
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Farleigh

**Summary:**
Farleigh (pronounced as Far-lee ) is a through station and minor terminus on the Esterfield Branch .

**Full Content:**

Farleigh Entrance Interior Platform View 1 Platform View 2 UoB (Avian Studies) UoB (Life, The Universe & Everything) Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone FAR G Station headcode Dispatching J Yes (1 slot) P1-2 Electrification Line Yes Esterfield Branch Station Information Location Farleigh District Zone - Platforms 2 Tracks 2 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station James Street 0.36 miles / 579 metres Airport West 1.83 miles / 2.95 kilometres Terminus Rosedale Village 0.99 miles / 1.59 kilometres Esterfield 2.02 miles / 3.25 kilometres Preceding depot Following depot Farleigh Depot (Road 2) Esterfield Mainline Depot Farleigh (pronounced as Far-lee ) is a through station and minor terminus on the Esterfield Branch . It is served by Waterline services to Newry , Benton and Esterfield ; and terminus for Waterline services from Newry Harbour . This station was released along with Rosedale Village and Esterfield as part of the Waterline Extension in Version 1.10 . Contents 1 Station layout 1.1 Legend 2 Services 3 Station announcements 4 History 5 Trivia 6 Gallery 7 References Station layout [ ] G Concourse Exit; ticket gates & ticket machines B1 Platforms Lift & stairs to concourse Platform 1 ‚Üí Waterline to Esterfield ( RDV / EFD ) ‚ä£ Waterline terminating platform ‚Üê Waterline to Newry Harbour ( JST ) ‚Üê Waterline to Newry & Benton ( JST ) Platform 2 Lift & stairs to concourse Legend [ ] ‚Üê Eastbound ‚Üí Westbound ‚ä£ Terminal Services [ ] Platform(s) Previous station Route Next station 1 Airport West R014 to Esterfield Esterfield James Street R016 to Esterfield Rosedale Village R018 to Newry Harbour Terminus 2 Esterfield R014 to Newry Airport West Rosedale Village R016 to Benton James Street Station announcements [ ] Type Audio Platform https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:FARPL.mp3 https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:FARC.ogg https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:FARM.ogg https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:FARWL.mp3 https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:FARE.ogg Please note: iOS and iPadOS do not natively support playing .ogg audio files and will show an error. To play these files, consider using another device or convert them into supported formats such as .mp3. History [ ] 2022 7 August Sneak peek for Farleigh was released. "Taking you to the Far parts of the county on todays episode of #SneakPeekSundays! Coming soon to an SCR version 1.10 near you! " 27 August - Version 1.10 Farleigh added to the network as part of the Waterline extension , as a Waterline through station. Platform 1 is also used as for terminating services from Newry Harbour . Based on Surrey Quays station . New routes: R014 , R016 & R018 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 Missing announcements on Stepford Connect and Stepford Express have been added. Trivia [ ] This station is based on Surrey Quays station in London. Farleigh provides a connection to the nearby 'University of Benton', as seen underneath the station's signage. This made many people in the community think that this station would be located in the Benton area . The station turned out to be the first station past James Street . Even though the university is named after Benton, the location of it is very far east from Benton. It takes about 6 minutes from Benton to this station without delays. Some people speculated this station to be a terminus, since the unoccupied platform shown in this station's sneak peek also had a green signal and stop car markers. However it could have also meant the platforms are bidirectional or that there are more than one platform in that direction. It was revealed in V1.10 that Platform 1 is both a through and terminating platform, while Platform 2 is a through-only platform. This station took over the "J" headcode from James Street . Farleigh (J), as well as Esterfield (Q), Leighton West (K), Airport Terminal 2 (X) and Airport Terminal 3 (Z), do not have a letter in their name that is their station headcode . There is a road from this station leading to Airport Terminal 2 . There is another road connecting Upper Staploe to this station. If one walked from this station to there, it would be faster than taking a train. This also applies to walking from Rosedale Village to Water Newton which the starting point is in the same Zone G. When driving to Benton on a Stepford Connect or a Stepford Express train, the announcer on-board does not state that the player can change trains to get to Farleigh. In place of these announcements is dead air and the logs show that these files are missing, likely due to developer oversight. This issue has been fixed in Version 2.0 . Originally, this station was to replace James Street and James Street itself would be completely demolished [ 1 ] . Some players have complained about Platform 1 being the terminating platform instead of Platform 2, as trains terminating at Platform 1 causes delays for trains headed to Esterfield . Additionally, due to the timetable giving a whole minute from James Street to Farleigh despite both stations being very close to each other, trains behind would have to wait up to two minutes for the terminating train to unload passengers and turn around. There is a commercial building named "Far from leigh(ton)" near the station. As of Version 2.0 , only diesel trains are allowed to terminate here as the only route terminating here is R018 , where the starting point, Newry Harbour , is unelectrified. ## Station 30: Faymere

**Page ID:** 5665
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Faymere

**Summary:**
Faymere is a through station on the Stepford Main Line and the first station along the Llyn extension, introduced in Version 1.4 .

**Full Content:**

Faymere Entrance Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Bird's Eye View Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone FAY E Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) P1-2 Electrification Line Yes Stepford Main Line Station Information Location Leighton District Zone - Platforms 2 Tracks 4 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines No Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station Edgemead 0.7 mi / 1.1 km Westercoast 1.2 mi / 1.9 km Preceding depot Following depot - Faymere Green NB Depot Track Layout to Faymere Green TMD to Edgemead Faymere is a through station on the Stepford Main Line and the first station along the Llyn extension, introduced in Version 1.4 . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Leighton City , Leighton West , Rayleigh Bay , Edgemead , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea . This station was revealed to the public on 29 September 2019. Route changes: R037 ( Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City <> Llyn-by-the-Sea ) R038 ( Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City <> Westwyvern ) Now terminate at Leighton City. New route: R042 2023 6 March - Version 1.10.4 Dispatcher and Guard trainings are no longer held at Faymere and now in a seperate training map. 2024 8 July Sneak peek for Faymere's overhaul was released. Zooming along the up fast towards version 2.0! 12 August - Version 2.0 Station upgraded, station entrance is now on the ground with a station car park. A footbridge now connects the 2 platforms, with the platforms now coloured red. Track layout remains unchanged. Added Stepford Connect services to the Rayleigh Bay branch . New routes: R050 & R102 Trivia [ ] The Class 68 and Class 444 exclusive routes, R026 and R036 , as well as Stepford Express , skip this station via the bypass tracks that cross the middle of the station. Trains on R004 , R009 and R041 spawning at Faymere Green NB Depot will also use the bypass tracks to skip this station while deadheading to Edgemead . Before V1.5 , this station was not dispatchable, despite having OFF indicators. There are no services to Stepford Victoria at this station as they all go on the passing tracks, passengers should change at Edgemead or Stepford Central to go there. Oddly, this station has no ticket machines. Financial Quarter is an elevated through station on the Stepford Victoria Branch .

**Full Content:**

It is served by limited Stepford Connect services to Stepford Victoria and Stepford Airport Central ; and Metro services to Willowfield , Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford United Football Club , Berrily , Morganstown , Barton and Port Benton . History [ ] 2018 11 December Sneak peek for Financial Quarter was released, as part of Day 11 of the Advent Calendar. Sneak peeked Financial Quarter 31 December - Version 1.1 Financial Quarter added to the network as part of the Stepford Victoria extension, as an elevated Stepford Connect through station with 2 side platforms. New routes: R005 , R006 & R008 2019 28 April - Version 1.2 Added Stepford Connect services to the Whitefield branch . New routes: R022 & R023 2020 22 June - Version 1.6 Added Stepford Connect services to the Willowfield branch . New routes: R028 & R029 2021 28 November Sneak peek for Financial Quarter's overhaul was released. The sneak peeked Financial Quarter 5 December - Version 1.8 Station overhauled, new station building and platforms are more detailed. Now resembles London Blackfriars station and South Quay station in real life. Route removal: R022 No longer stops here. 2022 27 February - Version 1.8.2 New route: R045 27 August - Version 1.10 Added Stepford Connect services to Airport Terminal 2 . New route: R046 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 Financial Quarter is now managed by Metro instead of Stepford Connect ; Stepford Connect services are now limited. New routes: R136 & R137 Route removals: R045 & R046 No longer stops here. Trivia [ ] The station resembles South Quay station in real life. This station has step-free access. However, lift access is only available at the west entrance. This station was originally going to be named Willowfield before it was revealed. The name Willowfield was reused for the Willowfield extension in V1.6 . The new Willowfield station was comparatively far from this station compared to City Hospital and Beechley . (City Hospital was originally going to be called "Beechley") The CIS Boards at this station do not function properly yet for an unknown reason. This is the only station to be located above/on a body of water. Prior to V1.9 , Eden Quay also shared this trait, until its overhaul. This station is unique for its elaborate platform surface detailing. This can also be seen at Elsemere Junction . This station was originally a part of the Metro Loop but since the cancellation of Metro , it was instead reopened in V1.1 as a part of the Stepford Victoria Branch . The station's Metro branding has been criticized by players as being ill-suited, compared to the Stepford Connect branding used prior to Version 2.2 , especially the escalators going up to platform level. ## Station 32: Four Ways

**Page ID:** 24532
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Four_Ways

**Summary:**
Four Ways is a through station located in the Metro Core Section . It is located near the Stepford Connect Headquarters between Stepford Central and Stepford East .

**Full Content:**

Four Ways HQ Square Entrance 4 Way Junc. Entrance Concourse Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone FWY J Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) PA-B Electrification Line Yes Metro Core Section Station Information Location Stepford District Platforms 2 Tracks 2 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Service Information Preceding station Following station Stepford Central 0.6 mi / 1.0 km Stepford East 0.4 mi / 0.6 km Four Ways is a through station located in the Metro Core Section . It is located near the Stepford Connect Headquarters between Stepford Central and Stepford East . It is served by Metro services to Willowfield , Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , Stepford United Football Club , Berrily , Morganstown , Barton and Port Benton . Construction first began in Version 2.1.3, with its name being confirmed in the preview of the Version 2.2 trailer on an OFF indicator, released on 11 May 2025. A rather red train at a rather green station! 1 April - Version 2.1.3 Station construction began near the Stepford Connect Headquarters , with construction barriers set up. 11 May - Version 2.2 Four Ways added to the network as part of the new Metro operator, as a Metro through station. New routes: R002 , R006 , R008 , R021 , R023 , R027 , R030 , R031 , R034 , R130 , R132 , R133 , R135 , R136 & R137 5 August - Version 2.2.1 A poster named "Redefining travel" was added at Platform A, which won the first Community Spotlight hosted in May 2025. 'Redefining travel' from eseopuhasnewname Trivia [ ] Before its name was revealed, many players speculated that the station sneak peeked on 17 March 2025 and the construction site near the Stepford Connect Headquarters were the same station. Where the station had the name "_r W_". However, even before the sneak peek on 17 March, the name "Four Ways" had already been leaked. Due to the similarities and the four way junction nearby, many players believed that the construction site was Four Ways station. This station is one of the two stations to not have a sign with its name in the entire network , alongside Stepford High Street . This station has received criticism from many players for being a bottleneck between Stepford Central and Stepford East , as both of these stations have 4 Metro platforms while this station only has 2. However, this may simply be due to the popularity of Metro following its introduction in Version 2.2 , and this likely exceeds the intended capacity of the station. History [ ] 2017 16 December Greenslade added to the network, as a Waterline terminus with 2 side platforms; and a Tramlink through station. New route: R013 21 December New routes: R010 & Newry Harbour <> Greenslade 2018 21 April - Version 1.0 Route removal: Newry Harbour <> Greenslade Removed from the game. 2020 22 February - Version 1.4.1 Scenery near Greenslade was upgraded. Added OHLE for both Waterline and Tramlink . 2021 1 January - Version 1.7.1 Station overhauled, new station building and platforms for both Waterline and Tramlink , as well as scenery upgrades. Waterline platforms now form a single island platform. 5 December - Version 1.8 Greenslade is now dispatchable. 2023 6 March - Version 1.10.4 Greenslade is now part of the training map. Trivia [ ] The concourse is based off of Oxford station . The platforms may be based on Bromley North station in London. There is a train station in South-East London called ' Slade Green ', the opposite of Greenslade. Prior to The Big Update , this station had services to Newry Harbour . Now, passengers will have to change at Morganstown Docks for the nearest direct service to Newry Harbour. This was one of the first Waterline stations. This station was most likely named after someone with the Roblox username SirGreenslade, who was a Security Officer for SCR. A Security Officer is a former High Rank . SirGreenslade is now a QD within SCR. When Greenslade was electrified in V1.4.1 , the Tramlink tracks got electrification as well, making part of the community anticipating that Tramlink might be fully implemented in the future. However, former Product Developer Mattyx2013 later stated that the Tramlink tracks got the OHLE only because it would look bland if only the Waterline ones got the overhead line equipment. The scenery between here and Whitney Green was also updated in the aforementioned update. Before V1.7 , if players walked on the Tramlink tracks, they could have found 2 abandoned stations at the west of this station, namely Berrily Denton Road and West Berrily , and the tracks ended just after West Berrily. These 2 stations were demolished in V1.7. After the aforementioned update, the Tramlink tracks now run into an inaccessible tunnel right after passing this station. This station has a ramp to platform level. Because the station's name used to be censored in in-game chat, it is often referred to as 'Green Salad' by players, usually in a humorous vein. It is quite common to see Waterline trains here as R013 ( Benton <> Greenslade ) is a popular points and experience grinding route. In the training map introduced in Version 1.10.4, Greenslade is at both ends of the five training corridors. It is also the station showcased in the training map main menu. However, the training version of this map lacks a second set of points allowing trains from either platform to turnaround and return as Trainee Drivers are asked to leave the server upon completion of the route. Greenslade in the signalling map (V1.7.1-V2.1.5) Despite the upgrade giving it an island platform in V1.7.1 , the station was still displayed with side platforms on the signalling map. This was eventually fixed in V2.2.0 . ## Station 34: Hallam Square

**Page ID:** 17913
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Hallam_Square

**Summary:**
Missing information

**Full Content:**

Missing information This article is a stub , which contains incomplete information that may not be accurate. You can help the SCR Wiki by adding more information. Missing information This article is a stub , which contains incomplete information that may not be accurate. You can help the SCR Wiki by adding more information. Cancelled feature This article or section covers content that was once proposed, but was ultimately not released to the main game. These are considered cancelled features. Cancelled feature This article or section covers content that was once proposed, but was ultimately not released to the main game. These are considered cancelled features. Hallam Square The station prior to its demolition. Operational Information Served by (proposed) Station code HLS Service Information Preceding station Following station Stepford Victoria Stepford Central Hallam Square is a demolished Tramlink station located right between Stepford Victoria and Stepford Central . It had a level crossing and ran parallel to a road beside it. It also had a large square with a fountain and a big red building near the station. It is rumoured that it was demolished when the Big Update was released. The former location of the station is now surrounded by water body. Hallam Square and its surroundings were built by former developer, FirstManchester135 (now known as Midland_Meridian). The station was named after the builder, whose real name is Zack Hallam . Trivia [ ] In real life, there is a real Hallam Square located in Sheffield.

## Station 35: Hampton Hargate

**Page ID:** 4733
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Hampton_Hargate

**Summary:**
Hampton Hargate is a through station on the Stepford Main Line .

**Full Content:**

Hampton Hargate Entrance Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone HHG D Station headcode Dispatching - No Electrification Line Yes Stepford Main Line Station Information Location Morganstown District Zone - Platforms 4 (2 in use) Tracks 4 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines No Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station Benton Bridge 0.7 mi / 1.1 km Benton 1.5 mi / 2.4 km Upper Staploe 1.4 mi / 2.3 km Water Newton 2.6 mi / 4.2 km Hampton Hargate is a through station on the Stepford Main Line . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Benton , Leighton City , Leighton West , Edgemead , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea . AirLink and Stepford Express have 2 platforms here, but those are unused and they pass this station.
