History [ ] 2017 29 November Hampton Hargate was added to the network, as a major through station with 8 platforms, to serve Metro , Stepford Connect , Stepford Express and High Speed. New route: R003 2018 21 April - Version 1.0 Station overhauled, platforms reduced from 8 to 2. Now serves Stepford Connect only, with passing tracks on the side. Added Stepford Connect services to the Leighton Zone . Route change: R003 ( Stepford Town <> Winstree ‚Üí Leighton City ) Now stops at Rocket Parade and Leighton Stepford Road and terminates at Leighton City. New route: R004 31 December - Version 1.1 Added Stepford Connect services to Stepford Victoria and Edgemead . Route change: R004 ( St Helens Bridge <> Leighton City ‚Üí Edgemead ) Now terminates at Edgemead. New route: R009 2019 17 December - Version 1.4 Added Stepford Connect services to the Llyn-by-the-Sea branch. New routes: R024 , R025 & R026 2020 22 June - Version 1.6 Added Stepford Connect services to the Willowfield branch . New routes: R035 & R036 29 October - Version 1.7 Station overhauled, now has 2 side platforms for Stepford Connect and 2 side platforms for Stepford Express and AirLink . Both pass and do not stop here however. Added Stepford Connect services to Upper Staploe . New route: R039 2021 5 December - Version 1.8 Added Stepford Connect services to Leighton West . Route change: R039 ( Benton <> Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City ) Now terminates at Leighton City. New route: R044 2022 27 February - Version 1.8.2 New route: R045 Trivia [ ] This station was originally going to be a major interchange incorporating eight platforms serving Metro , Stepford Connect , Stepford Express and High Speed, but all except two platforms were removed completely, and now it is a small and quiet station. This might be because Benton and Morganstown are not far from this station, and having three major stations very close together would be unnecessary. This station is one of the stations that received a scenery upgrade in V1.7 . Before the scenery upgrade, there were buildings located next to the station. However, this was seen as a downgrade instead by players as the area around the station now lacks scenery with the update removing buildings near the station. This station is one of the stations that many players consider to have the worst scenery in SCR, as the roads here do not connect anywhere and are just cut off, and this station also does not have any foliage or buildings nearby. The only thing there is a car park. After the V1.7 upgrade, platforms were added for the AirLink / Stepford Express passing tracks. However, they are not in use and no platform numbers are given to them. Among them, the eastbound passing platform forms an island platform with Platform 2. However, the eastbound passing side is fenced off as passengers are not supposed to enter. The westbound passing platform is inaccessible as the station footbridge is not connected to it, it also lacks any proper entrance. Although Morganstown can be seen from here with a high enough render distance, there is no direct link between them, so passengers have to go either via Benton or Leighton Stepford Road to get there. It is speculated that this will not be the case in Version 2.3 due to Stepford Connect getting routes to Westwyvern via Morganstown There is a siding east of this station, which is Hampton Hargate Siding , but trains cannot go to this station from there. There is also a track at Platform 1 that branches into the siding, likely for the future " Return to depot " feature. Despite not stopping here, Metro has an announcement for this station. The same applies to Leighton Stepford Road . ## Station 36: Hemdon Park

**Page ID:** 13394
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Hemdon_Park

**Summary:**
Hemdon Park is a small through station located along the Willowfield Branch . Metro services to Willowfield , Stepford Victoria , Stepford United Football Club , Berrily and Barton call here.

**Full Content:**

Hemdon Park Entrance Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Platform View 4 Bird's Eye View Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone HPK A Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) P1-2 Electrification Line Yes Willowfield Branch Station Information Location Stepford District Zone - Platforms 2 Tracks 2 Accessibility Step-free access via ramp & lifts Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station Willowfield 1.22 miles / 1.96 kilometres Beechley 1.54 miles / 2.48 kilometres Preceding depot Following depot Willowfield Mainline Depot - Track Layout to Willowfield to Beechley Hemdon Park is a small through station located along the Willowfield Branch . Metro services to Willowfield , Stepford Victoria , Stepford United Football Club , Berrily and Barton call here. Opened in Version 1.6 and overhauled in Version 2.1 , Hemdon Park station is located in a small town with tall buildings around, with a small park with a fountain nearby. It features 2 short side platforms which cannot accommodate most trains longer than 5-cars. Situated next to the station is the Beechley Royal Upholstery House commercial building . This station has step-free access to all platforms since Version 2.1. Prior to the station's upgrade, the Hemdon Park Rangers stadium was located near this station. Contents 1 Station layout 2 Services 3 Interactive map 4 Station announcements 5 History 6 Trivia 7 Notes 8 Gallery 8.1 Prior to Version 2.1 8.2 Prior to Version 2.2 Station layout [ ] Stopping Passing G Platforms Platform 1 ‚Üí Metro to Stepford Victoria , Stepford UFC , Barton and Berrily ( BCY ) ‚Üê Metro to Willowfield ( WFD ) Platform 2 Legend ‚Üê Eastbound ‚Üí Westbound G Platforms Platform 1 ‚Üí Stepford Connect to Whitefield , Port Benton , Westwyvern & Llyn-by-the-Sea ( BCY ) ‚Üê Stepford Connect to Willowfield ( WFD ) Platform 2 Legend ‚Üê Eastbound ‚Üí Westbound Services [ ] Platform(s) Previous station Route Next station 1 Willowfield R028 to Stepford Victoria Beechley R030 to Berrily R031 to Stepford United Football Club R133 to Barton 2 Beechley R028 R030 R031 R133 to Willowfield Willowfield Interactive map [ ] Station announcements [ ] Type Audio Platform https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:HPP.ogg https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:HPC.ogg [ note 1 ] https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:HPM.ogg N/A N/A Please note: iOS and iPadOS do not natively support playing .ogg audio files and will show an error. To play these files, consider using another device or convert them into supported formats such as .mp3. History [ ] 2020 22 June - Version 1.6 Hemdon Park added to the network as part of the Willowfield extension , as a Stepford Connect through station with 2 side platforms. New routes: R028 , R030 & R031 2024 24 December - Version 2.1 Station overhauled, with new scenery and full step-free access to the station. Platform layout remains the same. Now based on Ashley Down station . 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 Hemdon Park is now managed by Metro instead of Stepford Connect ; Stepford Connect no longer serves this station. New route: R133 Trivia [ ] The station is based on Ashley Down station . Prior to V2.1 , the station was based on Reading Green Park station . Prior to Version 2.1 , Hemdon Park was not fully step-free due to the lack of lifts to access Platform 2. It was one of three stations in the game that were not fully step-free, with the others being Eden Quay and Aslockby . This station, along with Willowfield , was not previewed before V1.6 . This station does not serve many routes unlike Willowfield and Beechley . Despite this, it is not considered a limited service station. This is the only station along the Willowfield Branch to have a name that was not used in the past, as both Willowfield and Beechley were planned to be served by Metro then. The old Willowfield is now Financial Quarter and the old Beechley is now City Hospital . After Version 2.2 , all Stepford Connect routes ( R032 , R035 & R036 ) now skip this station. This station's platforms are slightly shorter than the length of most 5-car trains. When they approach the station, the announcer will state that the doors of the rear coach will not open. This also happens at Woodhead Lane , New Harrow , Elsemere Pond and East Berrily . This station, Ashlan Park , and Beaulieu Park are the only stations in SCR to have "Park" in their name. This station is the Beechley Royal Upholstery House, a commercial building along the Willowfield line. Despite the name, the Beechley Royal Upholstery House is not at Beechley . Humorously, its name abbreviates to "BRUH." The name "Hemdon Park" may be a reference to "Hampden Park," a football stadium in Glasgow, UK. Glasgow also has a football club called Rangers F.C.. Just north of this station, there is a line of trees and a bridge over nothing with a right of way for a rail line that leads to a stop with grass platforms and no name. Innovations Director BanTech stated that this line is meant to be similar to an old and abandoned railway, similar to the unused track beds at Beechley . This could also be a reference to the Beeching Axe . There is a road that leads to Stepford UFC station from here, albeit not directly as the road floats above the actual road of said station. Notes [ ] ‚Üë This announcement was used in-game before the introduction of Metro , however, is no longer used. New route: R103 Trivia [ ] This station mainly resembles Eastham Rake , aside from the passenger bridge and the tunnel at the eastbound end of the station. Ironically, considering both stations end with ‚ÄòRake‚Äô. Along with Woodhead Lane and Westercoast , the level crossing is not functional and will stay lowered even if there is no trains. There is a small path next to the level crossing to cross platforms. Although it has not been confirmed, players speculate that this station was named after "Haughton Foundry", the group that created the game "Mind the Gap". This group was created by yrrebRBLX , one of the ex- PDVs at SCR who modernised Stepford Central . This station was one of few across the network to have a red National Rail logo outside the main entrance of the station. This was replaced when Stepford Connect was rebranded. As of V1.8 , this station is classified as a limited-service station. In the training map introduced in V1.10.4, Houghton Rake is one of the two through stations with Elsemere Pond . History [ ] 2018 5 December Sneak peek for James Street was released, as part of Day 5 of the Advent Calendar. I sense a theme going on here... Promise we've done more than just stations and routes üòÇ here's Day 5: James Street on Waterline extension ‚ùÑÔ∏è 31 December - Version 1.1 James Street added to the network as part of the Waterline extension , as a Waterline temporary terminus in a trench with 2 side platforms, only Platform 1 is used. New route: R014 2020 22 June - Version 1.6 Buffer added at the end of Platform 1 to prevent trains entering the tunnel and getting despawned. 2022 31 July Sneak peek for James Street's overhaul was released. Bet you weren't expecting this many station sneak peeks, but yet here we are, for another instalment of #SneakPeekSundays! 27 August - Version 1.10 Station overhauled, now located fully underground with an island platform. Now a limited-service Waterline through station. Station headcode removed, as James Street is no longer a terminus. J was taken by Farleigh . Signal Zone moved from Zone F to Zone G . Added Waterline services to Newry Harbour and Farleigh to Esterfield . Route removal: R014 No longer stops here. New routes: R016 & R018 Station models [ ] Original terminal station [ ] Prior to Version 1.10 , the station was the terminus of a branch from Cambridge Street Parkway , infamous for its outdatedness. It was also the site of a long-awaited extension with the tracks continuing past the station into tunnels. Before the addition of a buffer at the end of platform 1 in V1.6 , if a Driver attempted to go beyond the station or overshot the platform their train would be deleted immediately with a message saying "Invalid track detected". The station was also humorously viewed as cursed or creepy by some people, since it was left virtually untouched from its release unlike many other stations on the network. This was also due to the fact that the surrounding area lacked any form of scenery whatsoever, and that the area was quite remote from other parts of the county. The station was also placed in a trench. The station also only saw one service stopping, that service being R014 . This led to the train frequency being very low, as only few drivers chose to drive said route. Refurbishment [ ] James Street was refurbished in V1.10, which involved replacing the old station model in the old trench with a new underground station, adding a non-usable siding beyond the station towards Farleigh, and building a ticket office and new stairs and lifts down to the platform level from the surface. The station was also fitted with CIS Boards . The station entrance now resembles Farringdon station 's Barbican entrance, while the station itself resembles London Paddington's Elizabeth line station , which can be seen from the lights' designs above the platform. [ 1 ] The services serving the station were changed to be two new routes, R016 and R018 , with the original service, R014 , being changed to now skip James Street. This also made it the first and only Waterline route to skip any stations. Trivia [ ] Easter Egg Before V1.6 , the Waterline platform signs at Benton did not mention this station. In Liverpool, England, there is a station with the same name on Merseyrail's Wirral Line. Next to the station entrance, in an alleyway between a white building and a brown wall, there is a text saying " GREEISM WAZ HERE! " with 2 green paint products lying on the floor. These paint products seem to be manufactured by " Gree's Paint Factory ", as it says on the left capsule. Greeism was one of the Platform Managers , who helped with the surrounding scenery for the update. In V1.10 , James Street is no longer a terminal station, therefore its headcode "J" was moved to Farleigh . There is a siding near this station with a not-in-service Class 730/0 parked in it, though no trains can spawn there as it is occupied and too short for another train. Players thought that this siding would be a new spawning point for trains due to a sneak peek showing James Street inside of the Class 730, however this was not the case, and the siding is purely decorative. This was evident before Version 1.10 was even released due to the fact that in the sneak peek, signal D183 is shown as red, even though there is no other train inside James Street. Although the network map shows James Street as a limited-service station, the Waterline operator map shows James Street as a regular-service station on the Esterfield Branch . According to Product Developer tpx_jm, this is to show clearly that there are services that skips James Street on the network map . Though because 2 of the 3 routes stop at this station (and not less than 50% of routes), this station is not shown as limited in the Waterline operator map. This station was supposed to be demolished and replaced by Farleigh , according to Mattyx2013 . This would've made it the second station to ever be demolished, the other being Winstree [ 2 ] . This did not happen for unknown reasons and Farleigh is now the next stop eastwards on the Esterfield Branch . Excluding Metro stations, this is one of two fully underground railway stations, the other being Airport Terminal 1. In V1.10 , Airport Terminal 2 was rebuilt above ground, while James Street was rebuilt below ground. Prior to V1.10 , if the player's render distance was high enough, they could see a purple building with an ATC tower west of the station, which was the building of Airport Terminal 2 . After V1.10, players can directly walk from and to Airport Terminal 2 via road which is about 0.21 miles away. The tunnel section between this station and Airport West is located right under Airport Terminal 2 . According to Mattyx2013 , he designed a station model intended for Whitefield Lido at first, but then the model was changed to be used at James Street instead. [ 2 ] However, the model was never used, with many users speculating the current look of the Airport area being the reason for that. Between 1.6 and 1.9.7 the lights at the entrance to the station were painted in the old Waterline colours. The aforementioned Sneak Peek , showing the station without any buildings The original sneak peek of this station for 1.1 showed it without the surrounding buildings. Before V1.10, on the other side of the tunnels, the tracks would turn red (apparently to remind BanTech to replace them) and split into four tracks, before going to an unnamed station. ## Station 39: Leighton City

**Page ID:** 4738
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Leighton_City

**Summary:**
Leighton City is a major through station and terminus located at the southern end of the former Leighton Zone .

**Full Content:**

Leighton City Main Entrance 1 Main Entrance 2 South Bridge 1 South Bridge 2 Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Platform View 4 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone LTC D Station headcode Dispatching T Yes (2 slots) P1-4 , P5-6 Electrification Line Yes Stepford Main Line Station Information Location Leighton District Zone Leighton Zone Platforms 6 Tracks 6 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines No Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Terminus (From Leighton West or Edgemead ) Leighton Stepford Road 0.4 mi / 0.6 km Stepford Central 11.8 mi / 19.0 km Terminus (From Leighton Stepford Road ) Leighton West 0.4 mi / 0.6 km Edgemead 1.6 mi / 2.6 km Westercoast 3.8 mi / 6.1 km Westwyvern 7.3 mi / 11.8 km Northshore 8.4 mi / 13.5 km Llyn-by-the-Sea 9.0 mi / 14.5 km Leighton City is a major through station and terminus located at the southern end of the former Leighton Zone . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Benton , Leighton West , Rayleigh Bay , Edgemead , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea ; and Stepford Express services to Stepford Central , Newry Harbour , Newry , Benton , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea . Contents 1 Development history 1.1 Version 1.0 & Version 1.1 1.2 Version 1.4.1 1.3 Version 1.8 2 Station layout 2.1 Legend 2.2 Notes 3 Services 4 Station announcements 5 History 6 Trivia 7 Gallery Development history [ ] Version 1.0 & Version 1.1 [ ] Leighton City was released as a temporary terminal station. However it was designed for through services, which finally was extended in Version 1.1 , when the station was used for services to and from Edgemead . Despite being called "Leighton City", it was not at all connected to Leighton Stepford Road nor Rocket Parade via road, and the only thing that would make one think is that it was actually in a city is that the platforms were underground. Version 1.4.1 [ ] As part of Version 1.4 , Express was released with R077 stopping here. In addition, this station was also supposed to be redesigned in this update, but it did not fit in it. Hence the redesigned station was instead released in Version 1.4.1 . Version 1.8 [ ] Leighton City was overhauled with an increase to 6 platforms and became the main station of Leighton, as well as now being above ground. All Stepford Connect and Stepford Express services that terminated at Leighton Stepford Road now terminate here instead, as well as all services that skipped Leighton City no longer doing so. However, AirLink services still terminate at Leighton Stepford Road. New route: R004 31 December - Version 1.1 Added Stepford Connect services to Stepford Victoria and Edgemead . Route change: R004 ( St Helens Bridge <> Leighton City ‚Üí Edgemead ) Now terminates at Edgemead. New route: R009 2019 8, 9 & 15 October 3 sneak peeks for Leighton City's first overhaul were released. Welcome to... Leighton City? That's right! Leighton City has had an upgrade, a very modern one This will be released with the extension For those wondering, this is the reason for the bend in one of the platforms üôÇ Time to make the most of the old Leighton City üòõ 17 December - Version 1.4 Added Stepford Connect and Stepford Express services to the Llyn-by-the-Sea branch. Platform walls are more detailed with seating added. 22 June - Version 1.6 Added Stepford Connect services to the Willowfield branch . New routes: R035 , R036 , R037 & R038 2021 3 October Sneak peek for Leighton City's second overhaul was released. The next station to get a complete overhaul! Coming soon to v1.8! But where is it? ü§î P.s. the Bodin sign is just a standard advert. It isn't a clue! üòõ 5 December - Version 1.8 Station overhauled, now owned by Transport for Stepford . Platforms increased from 2 to 6 with Platform 3 & 4 being terminating platforms. Took the major terminus role from Leighton Stepford Road . Added Stepford Connect services to Upper Staploe and Leighton West . New routes: R003 , R037 , R038 , R039 , R043 , R044 , R076 , R078 , R080 , R081 & R082 18 December - Version 1.8.1 New route: R045 2022 25 April - Version 1.8.4 5 car Stop Marker adjusted to be 5-6 instead. 15 May - Version 1.9 Added Stepford Express services to the Newry branch . New routes: R083 , R084 , R085 & R086 2023 17 July - Version 1.10.8 HST & Class 80x stop markers added to all platforms. 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 All platforms extended to accommodate for longer trains. Added Stepford Connect services to the Rayleigh Bay branch . New route: R101 12 September - Version 2.0.1 Platform 3 & 4 can now serve through services if Platform 1-2 & 5-6 are full. 24 December - Version 2.1 New route: R088 Trivia [ ] This station is based on East Croydon . Prior to V1.8 , this station was based on City Thameslink . Prior to V1.4.1 , this station was based on Charing Cross (Glasgow) . Coincidentally, Airport West was previously based on City Thameslink and is now based on Charing Cross (Glasgow) . This station was originally going to be called "Leighton", which can be seen from the station signs prior to The Big Update . Although "city" is in its name, Leighton City didn't look like a city before V1.4.1 , as the only scenery was a street with a building. Before V1.1 was released on New Year's Eve of 2018, this station served as a terminus for trains from St Helens Bridge on R004 The sign located at the end of the platforms until V1.1 Before Version 1.1 , if any train proceeded past the sign that read " LINE CLOSED - DO NOT PROCEED " at the end of the platform, the train would be despawned automatically and the player would have been ejected. The same currently applies to the Platforms 3 and 4 at this station and other stations with platforms that have no buffers for terminating having the same trait. It also used to happen at James Street , but a temporary buffer had been installed there until the James Street Extension was released in V1.10 . Leighton Stepford Road used to have this trait as well before its Stepford Connect and Stepford Express terminus function was replaced by this station. Prior to V1.8 , this station was one of very few stations in the game to be underground, along with Airport West , Airport Terminal 1 and Airport Terminal 2 ; this was also the only non-airport and Stepford Connect underground station in the whole SCR network . When this station was a terminus before V1.1 , it was planned to serve Stepford Central -bound trains, but the idea was turned down, and trains terminated from St Helens Bridge instead. This changed in V1.8 , as the station is now the principal station in the Leighton Zone . Before V1.1 , it was not possible to dispatch at this station, and Platform 2 was unused. Platform 1 was used as a temporary terminating platform, which is similar to James Street before the extension opened in V1.10 . If one tried to make the old TTS voice on-board announcements for this station, they will have to use "Laighton City" instead of Leighton City to get the voice similar to the one in game. This is because when "Leighton City" is used, the voice says "Lee-ton". This is the same with Leighton Stepford Road . This station got its first upgrade in V1.4.1 . The terminating junction was also removed, meaning it was no longer possible to terminate at this station. After the second overhaul to the third generation in V1.8 , trains are able to terminate here again. This station was considered to be one of the worst-looking stations before its first upgrade. An advertisement for West Benton Pet Supplies was once placed on the Stepford Connect Information Board. However, it was removed in V1.8 , along with the one at Whitefield Lido . The ad can still be seen at Whitefield and Starryloch . The platform walls of the second generation station were similar to the ones at Airport West . Managing Director Charlie_RBX previewed this station again on 3 October 2021, with the station being handed over to Transport for Stepford and the number of platforms being tripled to six. Some people thought that the upgrade would be Westwyvern . Some people had once thought that due to the size of the station, Leighton Stepford Road might be closed and replaced with this station. However, another sneak peek released later on 14 November 2021 debunked such theories. Many players are confused as to why Leighton City was revamped as they claimed that the overhaul has no legacy to its second generation upgrade, and that the station was perfectly fine at its previous state. After the V1.8 revamp, all Stepford Connect and Stepford Express services that used to terminate at Leighton Stepford Road now terminate here instead. In addition, all Stepford Express services that passes through this station now stop here. Before that, R077 was the only route that stopped here. However, two AirLink routes, R056 ( Leighton Stepford Road <> Stepford Airport Central ) and R057 ( Leighton Stepford Road <> Airport Terminal 3 ), still terminate at Leighton Stepford Road instead of terminating at Leighton City despite the latter station being the new main station in the Leighton area . After the V1.8 update, this is one of the two stations where trains from both directions can terminate at the same platform, the other one being Edgemead . Previously, Leighton Stepford Road also had this trait before most terminating services were moved to Leighton City. Despite the station being handed over to Transport for Stepford , dispatchers working at this station were still given the Stepford Connect dispatcher uniform , instead of the generic SCR version used on stations managed by Transport for Stepford . This is possibly because Leighton City used to be owned by Stepford Connect before its upgrade in V1.8 , and it was simply an oversight from the developers. This was fixed in V1.9 . Despite being a major station, there are no ticket machines available for passengers anywhere in this station. This station, along with Leighton Stepford Road , Leighton West and Edgemead , are four terminating stations that are next to each other without any through stations in between. From V1.8 to V2.0 , this was one of the five multi-line through stations that were always stopped at by every route that approached it, with the others being Stepford Central , Benton , Newry and Stepford Airport Central . However, this became untrue with the arrival of R100 , where trains exiting Leighton Depot skip this station to go directly to Edgemead . Only three Stepford Express routes do not stop here, with those being R075 , R079 , and R087 . This means that this station could be considered as the operator's transport hub. In V1.8 , this station became notorious for its frequent signal failures (Signals S355 and S357), which is caused by the system thinking another train is still inside the block when it has already left. This caused the signals to stay locked at red occasionally and cannot be manually changed by a Signaller . Because of this, if a signal failure was detected in a server, Supervisors ended up shutting them down to prevent disruption. According to then- Community Manager tjh44, the root cause of the bug was not really known by the developers at the time, and the problem was clearly not a quick and easy fix. In V1.9 , this bug was patched. The light version of the Network Map in V1.8 showed that no Stepford Connect services stopped at Leighton City (and Edgemead ) despite it stopping at both, this was possibly due to an oversight while adding Leighton West to the map. This was fixed in V1.8.4. This happened again with the V2.0 map, where Leighton City had completely disappeared from the dark version of the Stepford Connect map. This was later fixed. R100 ( Leighton West <> Rayleigh Bay ) skips this station if spawned at Leighton Depot to Edgemead , being the only route able to skip Leighton City. There is a parked Class 68 near this station. ## Station 40: Leighton Stepford Road

**Page ID:** 205
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Leighton_Stepford_Road

**Summary:**
Leighton Stepford Road , located in the centre of the former Leighton Zone , is a major through station and terminus on the Stepford Main Line .

**Full Content:**

Leighton Stepford Road Entrance Ticket Gates Concourse Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Platform View 4 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone LSR D Station headcode Dispatching R Yes (2 slots) P1-3 , P4-5 Electrification Line Yes Stepford Main Line Station Information Location Leighton District Zone Leighton Zone Platforms 5 Tracks 5 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Rocket Parade 0.5 mi / 0.8 km Water Newton 1.5 mi / 2.4 km Morganstown 4.7 mi / 7.6 km Stepford Airport Parkway 4.7 mi / 7.6 km Benton 5.7 mi / 9.2 km Terminus Leighton City 0.4 miles / 0.6 km Preceding depot Following depot Leighton Depot - Leighton Stepford Road , located in the centre of the former Leighton Zone , is a major through station and terminus on the Stepford Main Line . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Benton , Leighton City , Leighton West , Edgemead , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea ; Stepford Express services to Stepford Central , Newry Harbour , Newry , Benton , Leighton City , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea ; and AirLink services to Stepford Airport Central and Airport Terminal 3 . This station is a replacement for the former station Winstree , (although closer to Rocket Parade ) which was demolished in The Big Update . This station was upgraded in Version 1.8 along with the rest of the Leighton area . It is no longer the major terminus, but the station itself is still very large and AirLink services still terminate here. History [ ] 2018 21 April - Version 1.0 Leighton Stepford Road added to the network as part of the Leighton Zone and replacement for Winstree . As a Stepford Connect through station and terminus with 5 platforms. Resembles Manchester Oxford Road . Route change: R004 ( St Helens Bridge <> Leighton City ‚Üí Edgemead ) Now terminates at Edgemead. New route: R009 2019 16 September - Version 1.3.26 ( Five Million Update ) Added AirLink services to Stepford Airport Central and Airport Terminal 3 . New routes: R024 , R025 , R026 , R076 , R077 & R078 2020 22 June - Version 1.6 Added Stepford Connect services to the Willowfield branch . New routes: R035 , R036 , R037 & R038 29 October - Version 1.7 Leighton Stepford Road is now managed by Stepford Express . Added Stepford Connect services to Upper Staploe and Stepford Express services via Morganstown . New routes: R039 , R080 , R081 & R082 2021 14 November Sneak peek for Leighton Stepford Road's overhaul was released. As we‚Äôve been quiet recently‚Ä¶ we thought we'd give you a bonus sneak peek this weekend for your patience! Another station upgrade coming to v1.8! 5 December - Version 1.8 Station overhauled. Now based on Haymarket station . Stepford Connect and Stepford Express no longer terminate here, but it remains a major through station for them and a terminus for AirLink . Added Stepford Connect services to Leighton West . Route removals: R037 , R038 & R081 No longer stop here. Route changes: R003 ( Stepford Central <> Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City ) R039 ( Benton <> Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City ) R076 ( Stepford Central <> Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City (via Benton ) ) Now terminate at Leighton City. New route: R044 Bug : Buffer at Platform 1 does not despawn trains. 18 December - Version 1.8.1 New route: R045 2022 25 April - Version 1.8.4 Bugfix : Buffer now despawns trains properly. 15 May - Version 1.9 Added Stepford Express services to the Newry branch . New routes: R083 , R084 , R085 & R086 27 August - Version 1.10 Platform priorities added, allocation is no longer randomised. RP P1 ‚Üí LSR P2, then P3 LC P3-4 ‚Üí LSR P4, then P5 LC P5-6 ‚Üí LSR P5, then P4 2023 17 July - Version 1.10.8 Class 80x stop markers added to Platform 2-5. 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 All platforms extended to accommodate for longer trains. Poles on the platform have been recoloured from Stepford Express pink to black. 24 December - Version 2.1 New route: R088 Trivia [ ] This station is based on Haymarket station in Edinburgh, Scotland. Before V1.8 : This station resembled Manchester Oxford Road station in Manchester, England . On some occasions, when Platform 1 was already occupied by an AirLink or Stepford Express train, trains could terminate on Platform 2, and if both Platforms 1 and 2 were occupied, trains could terminate on Platform 3. This happened very rarely though. This station was once the only through station in the game in which trains could terminate on every platform and from both directions, with platforms having Stop Markers at both ends. With the trait now replaced by Leighton City and Edgemead . This station was an overground station. Every route that approached this station stopped here, but since Leighton City became the major station at Leighton after that version, this is not the case anymore. Although the 5 car variant of the Class 43 is able to go on R076 when it terminated here, due to the length of Platform 1, the driver needed to stop very close to the buffer or else they could not open the doors and complete the route. Players could walk to Rocket Parade , but not Leighton City Like Elsemere Junction , this station used to owned by Connect before V1.6. After V1.8: Players can now walk from here to Leighton City . However, they can no longer walk to Rocket Parade . All Stepford Connect and Stepford Express services terminating here previously now terminate at Leighton City instead. R056 ( Stepford Airport Central <> Leighton Stepford Road ) and R057 ( Airport Terminal 3 <> Leighton Stepford Road ) still terminate here as of V1.8 , instead of terminating at Leighton City despite the latter station being the new main station in the Leighton area . During V1.6 and V1.7 , when some eastbound Stepford Connect services still terminated here, they did not use Platform 1. This was to allow trains from Stepford Central or Benton to terminate and continue onto R037 and R038 to Llyn-by-the-Sea and Westwyvern respectively. Before V1.6 , R003 could terminate on Platform 1, since the latter routes did not exist. This station has the third longest name in the game with 22 characters, just 2 characters fewer than Cambridge Street Parkway in second. But the longest name is Stepford United Football Club with 29. In V1.6 , new signs without operator branding were added at this station, just displaying the station name. The same could be seen at Elsemere Junction . Both of these signs were replaced with Stepford Express signage and AirLink signage respectively in V1.7 . The destination on the trains used to display "Leighton Stepford Road" in The Big Update , then it was changed to just "Stepford Road" in V1.1 due to some trains not being able to fit the destination properly on the destination board, but in the Five Million Update , it was changed again to "Leighton Step Rd". This was the first station ever to have through and terminating platforms shared by more than one operator. In the Five Million Update , AirLink was extended to this station to celebrate the game reaching 5 million visits. Currently, this station is one of the 6 triple-line junctions alongside Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Benton , Elsemere Junction , and Airport Terminal 2 . However, unlike most triple-line and quad-line junctions, this station is not run by Network Rail or Transport for Stepford , being run by Stepford Express instead. This also applies to Elsemere Junction and Airport Terminal 2 , which are stations operated by AirLink . Platform 1 used to have an old buffer , but it was replaced in V1.6 . This is the same as Stepford Airport Parkway Siding . This station once had the National Rail Double Arrow symbol for the entrance signage prior to V1.8 . Before V1.7 , although this station served AirLink , it was not on the spawn list for AirLink , so passengers spawning here had to spawn from the Stepford Connect or Stepford Express spawn lists. This was fixed in the aforementioned update. Although the station is called "Leighton Stepford Road", the decals outside the station entrance before V1.8 displayed "Stepford Road". Moreover, it was then possible to walk under the station. In V1.8 , R081 ( Stepford Central <> Llyn-by-the-Sea (super fast) ) was changed to stop at Leighton City instead of this station, making it the only Stepford Express route that is able to skip this station. This makes R081 the only route (that does not come from Leighton Depot as an ECS) to be able to skip this station. A Class 755 which passed through the buffer After the station's overhaul in V1.8 , the buffer at the end of Platform 1 did not despawn trains even if the driver crashed into it, allowing trains to crash and even go through the wall behind it. However, the train would still be despawned by other messages instead of the usual "Buffers don't like to be eaten." . This was fixed in V1.8.4. This station, along with Leighton City , Leighton West , and Edgemead , are four terminating stations that are next to each other without any through stations in between. Between V1.6 and V1.7, neither any SCR operator , Transport for Stepford , nor Network Rail managed the station. The station was unbranded and very simple signage. This also applied to Elsemere Junction . In V1.10 , trains now enter Platform 2 first as random platform allocation at through stations that allow skipping caused SPADs as Signallers do not know what platform the train is entering, therefore unable to set the signal to proceed before the train reaches the platform; and trains from Leighton City now prioritise Leighton Stepford Road Platform 4 if they come Platform 3 & 4, and Platform 5 if they come from Platform 5 & 6, this is to allow two trains to enter Leighton Stepford Road smoothly without a train unexpectedly entering another platform and crossing the junction, causing a SPAD . The black stripes on the pillars at the station were pink prior to V2.0 , many people said that this makes the station look worse than before. This station shares the headcode "R" with Rayleigh Bay . The other headcode sharing pairs of stations are Port Benton and Stepford Airport Parkway (P), and Benton and Barton (B). Despite not stopping here, Metro has an announcement for this station. The same applies to Hampton Hargate . ## Station 41: Leighton West

**Page ID:** 18194
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Leighton_West

**Summary:**
Leighton West is a small terminus on the Leighton West Branch , located between Leighton City and Edgemead .

**Full Content:**

Leighton West Main Entrance Second Entrance Platform View Bird's Eye View Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone LTW D Station headcode Dispatching K No Electrification Line Yes Leighton West Branch Station Information Location Leighton District Zone - Platforms 1 Tracks 1 Accessibility Level access Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station Terminus ( From Edgemead ) Leighton City 0.4 mi / 0.6 km Terminus ( From Leighton City ) Edgemead 1.7 mi / 2.7 km Preceding depot Following depot - Faymere Green NB Depot Leighton West is a small terminus on the Leighton West Branch , located between Leighton City and Edgemead . It serves Stepford Connect services to Benton , Leighton City , Rayleigh Bay , Edgemead and Llyn-by-the-Sea . After a double-track triangle from Leighton City and Edgemead , the line is merged into a single track. The majority of the line is a single track except for a passing loop, allowing two trains to pass, expanding capacity on the line. Contents 1 Development history 1.1 Before opening 1.2 Extension preview and clarification 2 Station layout 2.1 Legend 3 Services 4 Station announcements 5 History 6 Trivia 7 Notes Development history [ ] Before opening [ ] The plans for the extension were released to the public on 22 January 2021, with a vote regarding which one should be built in the #voting channel on the official SCR Discord. The vote gained a total of 7,349 votes as of 5 December 2021 with 2,906 votes for the Stepford Connect extension and 5647 votes for the Waterline extension . Extension preview and clarification [ ] The sneak peek, revealed by Charlie_RBX on 22 August 2021 On 22 August 2021, a sneak peek of a Class 333 departing to Llyn-by-the-Sea from an unknown Stepford Connect station was released, which led to some people in the community believing this sneak peek could represent a new station, and that it seemed like the extension was built in favour of Stepford Connect , despite more votes for Waterline . However, others thought that it might also be possible that the developers had decided to do both extensions, though this was unconfirmed at that time. Many people have also said that the station resembles Colchester Town . Later, during the Developer Q&A on 23 October 2021, Charlie_RBX has officially announced that both extensions will be built, in which the Stepford Connect one will be included as part of Version 1.8 . The Waterline Extension , however, would be built in another future update as part of the huge overhaul for the Airport Zone . Version 1.10 eventually saw the release of the Waterline Extension . Apologies it has been a while everyone... Expect quite a lot in this channel over the coming weeks! üëÄ We have been working hard on so so much behind the scenes as we work towards v1.8. It is still a little way off but, in the meantime, we will do our best to keep you adequately sneak-peeked! Coming soon to an SCR near you 5 December - Version 1.8 Leighton West added to the network as part of the Leighton extension, as a small 1 platform Stepford Connect terminus. Based on Colchester Town station . New routes: R041 , R042 , R043 & R044 18 December - Version 1.8.1 Announcement change: The Platform announcement is now: https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:LWPNew.ogg instead of: https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:LWP.ogg 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 Added Stepford Connect services to the Rayleigh Bay branch . New route: R100 Trivia [ ] This station is based on Colchester Town station in Essex. This is possibly an homage to the nearby former Winstree station, which was based on Colchester station. Although this station has the word "Leighton" in it, this station does not have any road connections to the Leighton Zone . If using R041 and R043 , the driver is able to drive from Leighton City to Edgemead via this station and select routes that are available to those two stations. Upon the release of V1.8 , heavy congestion at this station was common due to the fact that many drivers flooded here to visit this new station. Most of the branch line to this station is a single line and has a low speed limit of 30 MPH, worsening congestion. Signals in the area were also affected by a bug that locks them to danger, making all traffic to and from this station come to a standstill if it occurs. This has since been fixed. This station, despite having 5 routes terminating here, only has limited train service as two of the routes ( R041 and R043 ) only serve the nearby Edgemead and Leighton City stations respectively, and are the shortest services in SCR. In addition, the size of it and the mostly one-track layout on the line leading to it makes this station look tiny with low passenger demand. This station is one of the five Stepford Connect stations which do not have a route calling at Stepford Central , the others are Millcastle Racecourse , Aslockby , Carnalea Bridge , and Rayleigh Bay . This is also the only station in Zone D that does not have a route calling at any stations in the Stepford Area. This station is one of the three stations to have one platform, along with Airport Terminal 1 and Carnalea Bridge . When the initial sneak peek for this station was released, many members of the community believed that the station would be named Westwyvern West, Hemdon West , or similar, based off the vaguely visible CIS Board in the background. This station, along with Leighton Stepford Road , Leighton City , and Edgemead , are 4 terminating stations that are next to each other without any through stations in between. Leighton West (K), as well as Farleigh (J), Esterfield (Q), Airport Terminal 2 (X) and Airport Terminal 3 (Z), do not have a letter in their name that is their station headcode . Prior to V2.0 , this was the one of the two stations with a speed limit of 15 MPH on the station approach, with the other being Newry at Platform 1. The disused platform, with an overgrown trackbed There is a disused platform next to Platform 1 with an empty and overgrown trackbed. Narratively, this suggests Leighton West was originally a 2-platform station, with Platform 2 disused likely due to low passenger demand. However, it is also likely that the disused platform is also taken from the station Leighton West is modelled after ( Colchester Town station ). This is the only station whose platform announcement was redone.
